Volunteer Army Burns Enemy Army Vehicles

(Beiping) The 11th Brigade of the 1st Army Corps of the Volunteer Army, led by Wang Lituo, repeatedly attacked the Gaoling Station and various gates on the Rehe border. On February 20th, it led more than 500 troops and made contact with an enemy motorcade of more than 300 people near Lijiapu, burning several vehicles, killing more than ten Japanese soldiers, and the rest abandoned their vehicles and fled east, capturing many supplies. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

(Beiping) Cai Ruoyu, commander of the 15th Route Army of the Volunteer Army of Tang Juwu, and Commander Wang Fengge gathered and prepared to depart from Fushun County, Liaoning Province, and will go to the Rehe border to carry out the war of resistance against Japan. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

The Jilin-Heilongjiang Volunteer Army Actively Launches

(Beiping) After the failures of Ding Li and others, the various troops of the Jilin-Heilongjiang Volunteer Army mostly dispersed in the mountains waiting for opportunities. Now the troops of Chang Shouxu and others of the Volunteer Army have launched in the Jilin-Heilongjiang border, occupying sixteen counties, preparing to transfer all the troops to attack Rehe. (Special dispatch on the 26th) (Beiping) From November of last year to the end of January of this year, Su Huaxuan, commander of the Northeast Volunteer Army, fought with the 8th Division of the Japanese Army in Dushan and other places a total of 32 times, often engaging in frontal assaults and hand-to-hand combat. Both sides suffered heavy losses. In total, more than 1,000 Japanese officers and soldiers were killed or wounded. Our officers and soldiers suffered 1,284 casualties. The unit is currently recruiting patriotic people in various counties to join the team, and has completed replenishment and continues to fight the enemy. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

North China Ambulance Team Will Depart

(Beiping) The North China Ambulance Team is scheduled to depart on March 1st before the day (Beiping) This morning, a telephone call from Lin Yu said that the Japanese army in Yuguan suddenly increased again for several days, and part of the Japanese army in Koumenkou retreated, the intention is unknown. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

The Naval Aviation Department Decides to Move from Shanghai to Xiamen 4

Chen Wenlin is Appointed as Director

(Nanjing) The Naval Aviation Department was originally located at Hongqiao, Shanghai. It was destroyed by the Japanese pirates' invasion of Shanghai last year and has not been repaired. The Naval Commander Chen Shaokuan, considering that Shanghai is not a suitable place for aviation practice, decided to move the Shanghai Aviation Department to Xiamen. He ordered the department yesterday to handle the completion of all machinery, equipment, documents, and events within a time limit, and wait for orders to send ships to transport them to Xiamen. He also telegraphed the new director Chen Wenlin to select outstanding officers and employees of the department and the previous Xiamen Naval Aviation Department, which was eliminated, to merge and reorganize them and report the results. (Special dispatch on the 26th) (Nanjing) Shen Dexie, Director of the Shanghai Aviation Department of the Navy, submitted his resignation to the Naval Department, saying that since he took over as Director of the Naval Aviation Department in the eighteenth year, he had strived to expand and build the foundation of naval aviation, hoping to strengthen national defense. For three years now, many plans have not been realized. Rather than delaying national defense, it is better to yield to someone more capable. Moreover, Dexie is currently affiliated with the Aviation Agency and has a lot of work to do, so it is difficult to兼顧兼顧 serve as Director of the Naval Aviation Department. The future is long, and there is time to repay the country. Naval Commander Chen Shaokuan approved the report and appointed Chen Wenlin as his successor, with the rank of Colonel. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

Current Events Commentary

Final Resolution from Guangzhou 5

Recently, due to Washington's expression of willingness to begin negotiations on war debts, as well as the conflict of interests between Britain and Japan in North China, relations between Europe and the United States have clearly become closer. The intricate and complex international political situation is also evidently gradually turning its direction. Under this kind of turning point, the League of Nations has also changed its attitude of maintaining [Japan's Far East policy] for the past two years, and on the 24th of this month, resolutely passed the report drafted by the Committee of Nineteen with a vote of [forty-two to one], giving Japan a stern reprimand and formally denying the [Manchukuo puppet state]. This resolute and stern attitude is truly enough to make the world feel refreshed.

The fundamental reason for the change in the League of Nations' attitude towards Japan still lies in the conflict of interests between the major powers. In other words, the various forms of international politics are actually a manifestation of the [internal contradictions of imperialism]. Therefore, we must not mistakenly believe that [justice has now triumphed over might] in the current international situation, nor should we mistakenly believe that [all the powers are now helping us]. However, if we truly have the determination to fight for national survival, then the current international situation is actually an excellent opportunity for our country to make a final and greatest determination to mobilize ourselves for self-rescue. The tragic struggle in the Rehe region has now begun. Coastal and riverine areas are all uneasy and apprehensive, with the possibility of being attacked and disturbed at any time. Under the current circumstances, our government should show its final and greatest determination and declare to the whole country a consistent policy, so that the people of the whole country can concentrate their strength to support the government. Remembering the aftermath of the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-95, foreigners said that this war was not a war between [China as a country] and Japan, but a war between [Zhili Province] and Japan. It was not even a war between Zhili Province and Japan, but a war between [Li Hongzhang alone] and Japan. Learning from this past mistake, we are deeply afraid that the tragic struggle in Rehe will eventually end in tragic failure under the enemy's strategy of [divide and conquer], and will ultimately become like the results of the January 28th Shanghai Battle.

This time, Acting Executive Yuan President Song Ziwen and Zhang Xueliang personally went to Rehe to inspect the front lines and boost morale. According to telegram reports, the morale of the frontline soldiers and people has been greatly boosted. This shows that the people of our country today are not a people who are willing to perish. It is only because the previous government was indecisive and unable to decide on war or peace that they wanted to save the country but could not find a way to do so. In his speech at the welcome meeting in Rehe, Song said, [The government will never give up the Northeast, and will never give up Rehe.] He also said, [When a strong robber comes to the door, the only way to survive is to defend ourselves by force.] If Song's firm statement can truly represent the government's attitude, then we dare to ask Chairman Jiang to temporarily entrust his responsibilities in Jiangxi to other senior officials and immediately go to the front lines to appease and encourage the troops. This will not only further boost morale and strengthen their determination to resist Japan, but also the people of the whole country will look up to the banners and cheer and jump for joy to jointly participate in the national revolutionary struggle under this kind of resolute action.

Although the country is in such a critical state, the difference between survival and destruction is imminent. Our people certainly cannot continue to wait passively. Under the current circumstances, we have resolutely determined that struggle is necessary to curb the aggression of Japanese imperialism, struggle is necessary to maintain our own survival, and only by carrying out an anti-Japanese imperialist national revolutionary war can we find a way out for our nation's survival. Therefore, our people today should unite and mobilize, use the power of the masses to strengthen the government's backing, and strengthen the government's will. At the same time, we must also use the power of the masses to enrich the front lines of national struggle. The bloody battle of more than a month on January 28th last year, although extremely glorious and tragic, ultimately relied on the single blow of a Korean to give it a powerful blow. Is it only the people who have lost their country who have suffered great pain, and whose will to resist is more determined and whose actions are more heroic? We earnestly hope that the people of the country will seize the opportunity to save the country before it perishes. Do not wait until the country has perished to try to save it, but there is no way to do so. Today's matter is only about struggle. Let the government awaken, and let the people of the country awaken.

Various Countries Will Implement Economic Sanctions Against Japan 6

(Nanjing) According to foreign news, Japan's rejection of the League of Nations' resolution and its dispatch of troops to attack Rehe actually violate the world's public consensus on peace. In order to prevent the Far East incident from affecting global warfare, if the Japanese army continues to attack Rehe and the scope of the war in North China expands, they will unanimously suspend trade with Japan, first to warn Japan's brutality, second to maintain world justice to help the invaded Chinese nation, and third to benefit their own countries, because Japan's industry and commerce have gradually progressed in recent years, and the industrial goods of major European and American countries have not only seen a decline in those transported to Japan, but even in economically backward countries, those who previously sold large quantities of goods from the United Kingdom and the United States have recently been competed with by Japanese industrial goods, and the number is not small. Therefore, in fact, suspending trade with Japan is also beneficial to the interests of major countries themselves. As for implementing Article 16 of the League of Nations' Covenant to block the Japanese economy, due to the mutual relations between countries, it is still the second step. (Special telegram on the 26th)

French Engineer's Collection of Books Donated to the Peiping Library 7

(Beiping) The late French engineer Pu Yiya, the former chief engineer of the Pinghan Railway, had a very rich collection of books during his lifetime. The United States Officially Supports the League of Nations 8

The State Department replied to the League of Nations' endorsement of the report

And expressed its participation in the League of Nations Advisory Committee

(Washington) The current U.S. Secretary of State Stimson and the future Secretary of State Hull today discussed all U.S. diplomatic and military affairs, and then the State Department sent a letter to the League of Nations, stating that the United States generally agrees with the League of Nations' conclusions on the Manchuria case. At the same time, Hull also made a brief statement to the public, arguing for the dignity of treaties and expressing his complete agreement with the League of Nations report. Regarding the League of Nations Advisory Committee, it is reported that U.S. Secretary of State Stimson claimed that he now believes that the United States should cooperate with it, and expects that future Secretary of State Hull will also have the same intention, because Hull has stated that he believes that any opportunity for international cooperation to solve important problems should not be missed.

The U.S. government's reply is in response to the League of Nations' invitation to the United States to endorse the views expressed in the report on the Manchuria case and to comply with them jointly. In addition to declaring its support for the League of Nations' conclusions, it also attached advice to China and Japan to resolve disputes peacefully. It first stated that the U.S.'s purpose in the situation arising from the Sino-Japanese dispute is generally consistent with that of the League of Nations, both aiming to maintain peace and resolve international disputes peacefully. In order to achieve this goal, the United States has tried to assist when the League of Nations is exercising its management power over disputes between the two member states, in order to jointly maintain peace. However, at the same time, it reserves the right to make its own decisions regarding methods and scope.

Then, it recounted that the League of Nations, based on the facts of the investigation, made its conclusions into a well-considered explanation, stating that the U.S. government generally agrees with these conclusions, and also said that the U.S. government expresses general agreement with the principles of resolution proposed by the League of Nations, which are in line with the treaties signed by the United States.

Then, it discussed the level of peaceful resolution, with rather euphemistic wording. It is claimed that one is due to the current tension of the situation, and the other is because this letter is actually a statement made by Stimson on behalf of the new government. It said that the two countries currently in dispute have long established friendly relations with the American people. The U.S. government sincerely hopes that both sides will see a way to make their policies conform to the needs and wishes of the League of Nations in view of the world public opinion that has now been clearly expressed, and hopes that disputes between the two countries will not be resolved by any means other than peaceful means.

This letter was drafted by two assistant secretaries of state, Humek and Rogers, with the assistance of Stimson. However, the fact that the League of Nations' invitation can be answered so quickly is enough to show that Roosevelt's attitude is completely the same as that of the Republican government. (National Telegram on the 25th)

(Washington) After Secretary of State Stimson and Hull discussed, they sent an important official document to the League of Nations regarding the U.S.'s position in the Sino-Japanese dispute, stating that the U.S. government's purpose in this dispute is mostly in line with the League of Nations' purpose, and their common purpose is to maintain peace and resolve international disputes by peaceful means. As for the declaration of the principle of not recognizing [Manchukuo] and the expression of attitude towards this issue, the League of Nations and the United States are in a common position. The U.S. government expresses general agreement with the principles of such suggestions based on the treaties it has signed. (Reuters telegram on the 25th)

Stimson and Hull Issue Joint Statement 9

(Washington) Today, the future U.S. Secretary of State Hull and the current Secretary of State Stimson met, and then told people that the scope of the talks was very broad, which is usually the case during the transition between the old and the new, and said that the opinions of the two were mainly based on compliance with treaties. The United States or any country should not be slack in complying with the words and spirit of treaties and taking care of international credit. Then, it was indicated that the two would meet with British Ambassador Lindsay and French Ambassador Crouta tomorrow, but the issues to be discussed would not be disclosed. According to reporters' exploration from other sources, the Far East situation will probably be discussed together with issues such as war debts and world economic recovery. Hull then stated that he believes that resolving war debts is indeed a definite element in encouraging world recovery, but it is only a part of it. Therefore, the future formal war debt conference is only a part of a large movement in which countries jointly seek economic recovery. He intends to follow a broad policy of international cooperation for all world events, hoping to accelerate the increase in international trade, resolve disputes between countries, and said that he may meet with Stimson every day before the government transition on March 4. (National Telegram on the 25th)

(Washington) It is reported that today, when Secretary of State Stimson and the next Secretary of State Hull held a meeting at the State Department, they have decided to issue a declaration. The declaration is currently being drafted. The general idea is to express cautious approval of the League of Nations' condemnation of Japan's Manchuria policy. The meeting between Stimson and Hull was held after receiving the notification from the League of Nations General Assembly, which stated that the League of Nations had passed a resolution inviting the Soviet Union and the United States to participate in the League of Nations' work to mediate the Sino-Japanese dispute. (Reuters telegram on the 25th) (Nanjing) According to diplomatic sources, the League of Nations Advisory Committee has officially invited the United States and the Soviet Union to participate. The United States believes that the facts and recommendations in the report are in line with the U.S.'s opinions, and that cooperation with the League of Nations is very possible. As for the Soviet Union, it will also take consistent action with the United States. (Central News Agency Telegram on the 26th)

Lord Lytton Again Calls for Sanctions Against Japan When the Time Is Ripe 10

The League of Nations Cannot Condone Japan's Reckless Actions

Hope the UK Fulfills its Treaty Obligations

(London) Lord Lytton said in a speech in Godalming today, referring to the Sino-Japanese dispute, that the time is now ripe for the League of Nations to declare the application of the sanctions methods contained in Article 16 of the Covenant, and he hopes that the UK can be prepared to fulfill its obligations under the treaty. He firmly believes that the solution he proposed is the only way to suit the facts. We must make Japan understand that the League of Nations cannot condone actions that violate the rules. More importantly, we must make Japan understand our sincerity in seeking solutions within the rules. (Reuters telegram on the 24th)

Japanese Government's Opinion After the General Assembly Passed the Report 12

Still Denying the League of Nations' Judgment

Repeatedly Arguing, What Good Is It?

(Geneva) The Japanese representative here published Japan's opinion on the League of Nations General Assembly report. In the conclusion, it denied many of the League of Nations' judgments, such as claiming that Japan did not exceed the scope of self-defense in Manchuria, [Manchukuo] was naturally produced, and Japan had not violated the League of Nations Covenant, the Nine-Power Treaty, or the Kellogg-Briand Pact, forcefully claiming that Japan had no territorial ambitions in Manchuria, and only wanted to make Manchuria a barrier to communist invasion of the Far East, etc., which is nothing more than deceiving people. In addition, it repeatedly slandered China's disorganization in order to obscure the world. (National telegram on the 26th)

(Tokyo) The main points of the statement submitted by the Japanese government to the League of Nations are as follows:

Part 1: Japan's Cooperation with the League of Nations. Japan has cooperated with the development and success of the League of Nations for more than ten years. China requested the League of Nations Council to deliberate on the Sino-Japanese issue, but the Japanese military action was a self-defense action against the Chinese military attack. The difference in opinion between the League of Nations and Japan occurred because the League of Nations lacked understanding of the Far East. Japan once requested the League of Nations to send an investigation team to understand the true situation of China, but the Committee's report cannot be used as a book sufficient to describe the truth of China. Therefore, Japan submitted a statement of opinion on November 18 last year, but the subsequent organization of the national situation was the organization of the Committee of Nineteen without Japan's consent. Later, in accordance with Article 15, Paragraph 2 of the Covenant, it drafted a resolution on reconciliation and the reasons, and Japan requested the deletion of the two sections that did not recognize Manchukuo from the resolution, and at the same time continued to negotiate with the League of Nations and submitted various proposals in order to discover compromise means, but to no avail. The Committee of Nineteen recognized that the third reconciliation was impossible and drafted the fourth report, which was submitted to the General Assembly on February 24 and passed despite Japan's opposition.

Part 2: Errors in the Report. It is a pity that the report uses the Lytton Report as its foundation to review the facts of the dispute. The report recognizes that China's boycott of Japanese goods after September 18 was a means of retaliation, but the matter will definitely have an impact on all countries related to China in the future. Also, the report states that Japan's military action on September 18 cannot be regarded as a self-defense action. The Japanese government denies the resolution that China's boycott of Japanese goods was retaliation. The report also said that the independence of Manchukuo did not occur due to the automatic will of the residents. This is the erroneous conclusion of the Lytton Report.

Part 3: Recommendations That Cannot Be Implemented. (1) When applying the principles of the Covenant and the Paris Treaty to abnormal situations such as China, it is strictly necessary to give it considerable flexibility. (2) The report recommends the withdrawal of the Japanese army, but the stationing of the Japanese army is not contrary to legal principles. The Japanese army is based on the Japan-Manchuria Protocol and has the responsibility to maintain the internal security of [Manchukuo]. (3) Although the report claims that the sovereignty of Manchuria belongs to China, Manchuria has not belonged to Chinese power since 1916. (4) Omitted. (5) The method of establishing a negotiation committee is contrary to Japan's claim that it does not allow any third party to interfere in the Manchuria issue. Therefore, Japan absolutely cannot accept such a proposal.

Part 4: Conclusion. The Japanese government is convinced that the Japanese military actions after September 18 were all within the scope of self-defense, and that [Manchukuo] was established by the automatic will of the residents of Manchuria. Therefore, the Japanese government believes that the actions of its army and the conclusion of the Japan-Manchuria Protocol do not infringe on the League of Nations Covenant, the Kellogg Pact, the Paris Treaty, or any other international treaty. [Manchukuo] is now promoting rapid development, and foreigners and Manchurian residents are benefiting from it. This proves that Japan's recognition of Manchukuo is a concrete fact that it is the only way to maintain peace in the Far East. (United Press telegram on the 26th)

Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs Prepares Steps to Withdraw from the League of Nations 13

Uchida Says It Can Be Completed Within Ten Days

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Uchida reported to the cabinet that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs can complete the necessary internal steps for Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations within ten days. (Reuters telegram on the 26th) (Tokyo) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has begun drafting a concrete plan to consult with the Privy Council regarding withdrawal from the League of Nations, which is divided into four parts as follows: (1) The notification to the League of Nations Secretariat regarding withdrawal; (2) The matter of amending the Treaty of Versailles due to the submission of the notification; (3) The obligations that the Japanese government should bear for two years after submitting the notification; (4) The handling of the Disarmament Conference, the Labor Conference, and other international conferences hosted by the League of Nations. Several days are still needed to complete the above four official documents. Therefore, it is estimated that the notification to the League of Nations will be made around March 10 to 15 after the cabinet decides to submit the consultation case to the Privy Council meeting. Also, due to the importance of issues such as the mandated territories, the Labor Conference, and the Economic Conference, the relevant provinces have been ordered to investigate as soon as possible. Some cabinet members advocate that the Labor Conference and the Disarmament Conference should continue to attend from separate standpoints. It is estimated that among the four disarmament representatives, Matsudaira, the ambassador to the UK, will stay until the end to observe the trend of the meeting. The other three representatives, such as Ambassador Sato, and the plenipotentiaries of the Army and Navy, Tatekawa and Nagano, will each return to their posts in their home countries. (Dentsu telegram on the 26th)

Matsuoka Yosuke Departs with Sorrow and Disappointment 16

Issuing a Self-Deprecating Lament on Departure

(Paris) Matsuoka Yosuke, the chief representative of Japan at the League of Nations, arrived here at 10:40 last night and will stay for several days before going to London. Other members of the Japanese delegation arrived here this morning. (Havas telegram on the 26th)

(Geneva) Matsuoka Yosuke, the chief representative of Japan, sent a telegram after leaving Geneva, which was immediately forwarded to the press to explain his feelings of farewell, saying: "When I left Tokyo earlier, I was determined to do my best to explain Japan's claims so that the people of Europe could understand our position and the difficulties we encountered. I wanted to avoid a conflict between the League of Nations and Japan so that Japan could continue to participate in the League of Nations. I was confident that this move was not without hope. Who knew that after March, this hope was completely destroyed. I left with emotions of distress and disappointment. I am not distressed for Japan, but for the League of Nations having made this hasty decision. This will inevitably prove after some time that the League of Nations will suffer more than Japan. I am even more saddened for China, because the actions of the League of Nations will not only fail to resolve the dispute, but will also add a confusing element to the situation in China, and Japan's struggle to stop the unrest will be even more obstructed from now on. I think that the only good thing about this move is that the Japanese people are becoming more and more united, and are more aware of the importance of the current difficult situation and the arduousness of Japan's responsibilities, and are even more determined to restore and maintain the peace and order in the Far East with all their strength. If the actions of the League of Nations can produce this unique effect, then Japan may be grateful to the League of Nations. Although, we still hope that this action of the League of Nations will not widen the divide between the East and the West. As for me personally, I have neither resentment nor fear, so there is no need to waste words. I have always had a hope that Japan will one day be understood by the world. When I leave Geneva, I silently wish that all member states of the League of Nations will be able to obtain enlightenment, and sincerely hope that the efforts of the League of Nations will be successful. What I am comforted by is that the representative of Siam abandoned the voting rights of the sub-resolution. Siam, as a country, is the only Asian country, except for Japan and [Manchukuo], that is truly complete and fully responsible, and has the desire and ability to be independent. As I leave Geneva, I would also like to sincerely thank all member states of the League of Nations for the work they have completed in the past seventeen months, the problems they are facing, and the problems they have encountered in the thirteen years since the League of Nations was established. Their efforts to try to solve the problems are commendable. I would also like to express my gratitude to the city of Geneva and its residents, because the residents of Geneva's style of discussion is deeply felt by the Japanese delegation and me personally." (Havas telegram on the 26th)

(Geneva) Japanese representative Matsuoka told a Reuters reporter before leaving for the Netherlands, referring to the passage of the report and recommendations by the League of Nations, that if I did not have the perseverance of an Oriental, I would definitely cry for it. Future historians will regard the cancellation of the Anglo-Japanese Alliance after the European War as one of the greatest tragedies of our time. He also said that Japan does not want to annex Manchuria. (Reuters telegram on the 25th)

Precarious Situation in Tianjin Under Provocation 17

Japanese Soldiers Dig Bunkers and Arbitrarily Arrest Pedestrians

Armed Japanese Soldiers Forcibly Attempt to Inspect Police Station

One Location at the Border Has Been Blocked

Japanese Soldiers at Tanggu Barracks Dig Tunnels

(Tianjin) On the southeast side of the Japanese garrison in Haiguang Temple, Japanese soldiers, on the avenue from Tianjin to Fengwo, dug bunkers resembling artillery emplacements. Two armed soldiers are stationed there in shifts. At 9 PM on the 25th, two people riding bicycles passed in front of the Zhongyuan Company in the Japanese Concession, and were arrested by Japanese soldiers and taken into the Japanese garrison. Pedestrians, witnessing this, suspected something was amiss and fled in droves. The Japanese police station immediately imposed martial law, which was lifted again at 10 PM. According to information leaked from Japanese residents, the Japanese garrison currently has fifteen tanks and two aircraft. When necessary, plainclothes teams will be unleashed into Chinese territory to create disturbances, and then the intersection of Tonghua Street in the Japanese Concession will be sealed off, and no one will be allowed to retreat back into the Japanese Concession under any circumstances. The Fourth Precinct of the First District and Sixth Precinct of the Public Security Bureau is not far from the Japanese garrison in Haiguang Temple. On the evening of the 24th, five armed Japanese soldiers suddenly attempted to enter the precinct to "inspect." The patrol chief, Zhao Yunpeng, immediately refused, saying there was nothing to see inside. The Japanese soldiers were aggressive and intent on provoking a conflict. Eventually, they were tactfully persuaded to leave by the security team. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

(Tianjin) Japanese soldiers arrested two of our protected policemen in front of the Zhongyuan Company on the evening of the 25th and released them at noon on the 26th. The Public Security Bureau has issued an order to all district teams that uniformed personnel are not allowed to pass through the Japanese Concession. At noon on the 26th, Japanese soldiers blocked the intersection between Xujie Street and Guangxing Avenue with a brick wall. On the evening of the 26th, Japanese soldiers, together with Japanese police, searched pedestrians. (Telegram on the 26th) (Tianjin) In recent days, many Japanese women and children have come to Tianjin from Beiping and Zhangjiakou. The Japanese Consulate has chartered the Tianjin Maru, scheduled to send them to Dalian on the morning of the 27th, from where they will transfer to ships eastward. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

(Tianjin) The Japanese military authorities here are now making every effort to fortify the defenses of the Japanese Concession. All streets and alleys connecting to the concessions are being blocked with barbed wire obstacles, and short walls made of brick and cement are being built in several locations. Thousands of sandbags are currently being filled in preparation for emergencies. All work is being done by Japanese soldiers. Residents in the Chinese-administered area are very apprehensive, but so far, no one has moved into the foreign concessions. (Reuters telegram on the 26th) (Tianjin) According to a telephone call from Tanggu, the Japanese garrison there is digging tunnels inside the barracks, strictly forbidding Chinese people from spying. It is not known where the tunnels lead, but it is speculated that they are heading towards the railway station. The Japanese military in the area has recently stepped up security measures, with many sentries patrolling at night, prohibiting pedestrians, creating a tense situation. Defensive fortifications are being built in many places with sandbags. The transport ship H-ji-ko Maru arrived from Lushun a few days ago carrying a large quantity of military supplies, all of which were rifles and bombs. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

U.S. Congress Prevents Financial Crisis 61

President Hoover is Considering It

Washington, 25th (National News Agency) After banks in Maryland closed for three days to prevent a run on deposits, the financial community in Washington was greatly shaken because it is only 40 miles from Baltimore and the banks in the two places are closely related. The Senate and House of Representatives of Congress immediately put Kushner's emergency banking bill on the agenda for discussion, and passed the bill today, authorizing national banks to provide financial assistance to state banks in times of financial emergency. It is currently under consideration by President Hoover. In addition, the Maryland legislature has a bill to limit the amount of withdrawals that bank depositors can make without prior notice, and it is expected that it will also be passed tomorrow. Both of these bills can prevent state banks from declaring another suspension of payments. The power to implement them is now in the hands of the U.S. President and the Governor of Maryland.

Washington, 25th (Reuters) There are over 6,000 banks in the United States, with total deposits of $17,000,000,000. The Senate and House of Representatives have passed a bill granting the Comptroller of the Currency the authority to place limited restrictions on withdrawals. This bill will become law upon presidential approval. This power is granted to the Comptroller of the Currency for a period of six months, which can be extended with the consent of the President and the Secretary of the Treasury. In practice, this bill directly grants temporary emergency powers to the Comptroller of the Currency, but state governments already have this power over state-chartered banks.

Chiang Kai-shek Issues Another Order for Fan Xiji to Eliminate Xu and He Bandits 64

Xu Bandits Gather in Tongjiang

He Bandits Flee in Disarray to Tianmen

Hankou Correspondence: Since the Xu bandits fled to northern Sichuan and the He bandits fled to western Hubei, forming two major forces, Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek immediately dispatched He Chengjun as the commander of the suppression campaign and Tian Songyao as the bandit suppression supervisor of the Sichuan-Shaanxi border region to pursue and block the Xu bandits. He also ordered Fan Xiji, the chief of the Hubei Provincial Security Department, to rush to Yichang to supervise the suppression of the He bandits. More than a month has passed since then. According to Tian Songyao’s telegram from Ningqiang on the 23rd, the bandits initially entered Sichuan with only five or six thousand men. In the past two months, they have collected various local bandits in the Sichuan-Shaanxi border area, such as Ren Weizhang, and seized group guns, increasing the number to thirty or forty thousand, with no less than ten thousand guns. They were organized into the pseudo Fourth, Ninth, and Twenty-fifth Armies, and there were also names such as Red Army, Pioneer Corps, Children's Corps, Red Guards, Militia, Guerrilla Squad, and Upper, Middle, and Lower Vanguard Squads. The bandit leaders are Zhang Guotao, the pseudo director of the Northwest Military Affairs of the Chinese Soviet, Xu Xiangqian, the pseudo commander-in-chief and army commander, Kuang Jixun and He Wei, the pseudo director of the General Political Department, Tao Changhao, the pseudo general director, Zhang Qinqiu, and the pseudo political commissars Zhan Fangcai and Gan Yuanjing. They committed arson and murder, showing extreme cruelty. After investigation, Tian's troops, although stronger than the bandits, felt a lack of bullets. The troops of Hu Zongnan and Liu Maoen, who were originally elite and belonged to Shaanxi suppression, were transferred to Gansu, leaving only Liu's troops to enter Sichuan, and the supplies could not be transported. A month ago, Shaanxi sent personnel to escort military rations to Sichuan, which took a month to arrive. The transported rations were eaten up by the transporters, as the road was dangerous and there were no residents. Northern Sichuan and southern Shaanxi are the most barren, and there is no food to buy along the way, so they have to fill their stomachs with military rice. Under these circumstances, the bandits were able to expand their strength through intimidation and enticement. Tian Songyao's telegram clearly shows that the situation is becoming increasingly serious. Tian recently sent a representative to Nanchang to meet Chiang Kai-shek and personally present everything. It is heard that Chiang instructed to re-telegraph Tian, instructing him to eliminate the bandits and prevent them from fleeing far away. At the same time, he also ordered Fan Xiji to be responsible for eliminating the He bandits. According to the latest news, Tian's troops have captured Bazhong and are advancing to suppress Tongjiang. Liu Cunhou and Liu Maoen's troops have also advanced to Moshitou, more than ten miles away from Tongjiang, and will launch a joint attack within days. As for the various units of the He bandits, except for a part that remained in Hunan, most of them have returned to the border of Hubei. The county seat of Wufeng was once lost, but the newly appointed county magistrate Sun Bin, specially appointed by the provincial government, telegraphed that he had risked his life to take office, seemingly indicating that the bandits had withdrawn from the county seat and had other plans. The Wang Bingnan unit of the He bandits was defeated by Fan Xiji in Xintang before, and fled to Shiziguan in Xuan'en. After sending teams to pursue and suppress them, they fled to Ximaping in Tianmen. Fan is supervising the troops to encircle and suppress them, and Xu Yuanquan has also sent troops to block them in various places to prevent them from going deep. (February 25)

Founding of the Hubei Provincial Air Force Creation Association 65

Xia Doutang, He Jingwu and others Elected as Directors and Supervisors

Hankou Correspondence: The Hubei Provincial National Air Force Creation Association held its inaugural meeting at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 1:00 PM on the 25th. Leaders from all sectors of the Party, government, military, gentry, business, industry, and academia attended enthusiastically. The presidium of the meeting included Ye Peng, Chen Daxun, He Jingwu, Su Taiyu, Pu Xinya, He Hengfu, Huang Yingzhong, Lou Botang, etc. Ye Peng was publicly elected as the general chairman, and reported the significance of the meeting, briefly stating that in modern scientific progress, the use of air force in war has suddenly increased in importance. Therefore, the outcome depends not on the quantity of the navy and army, but on the strength of the air force. Without an air force, there is no national defense. The Premier had already instructed in the past that, as the national crisis is pressing and the government's finances are difficult, the people should automatically create an air force. Saving the country is saving oneself. The turmoil of the roving bandits in the late Ming Dynasty shows that the wealthy were unwilling to contribute their wealth until the city was breached, but they still could not protect themselves. The image of national subjugation can serve as a warning. Next, He Jingwu, Fang Benren, He Hengfu, Zhou Xingtang, and others gave speeches, all of which were extremely poignant. After the speeches, the Refined Salt Association immediately donated 2,000 yuan on the spot, and the Security Joint Association donated 1,000 yuan. Then, He Jingwu read out the various proposals, which were unanimously passed by the entire audience: (1) The Provincial Air Force Creation Association is established today, with the general headquarters located at the Hankou General Chamber of Commerce. (2) Telegraph all counties and cities in the province and various groups in Wuhan to quickly establish branch associations. (3) Telegraph all provinces in the country to quickly establish National Air Force Creation Associations to unite and resist foreign aggression. (4) Pass the general association constitution. (5) The telegrams that have been sent are approved retroactively. (6) Pass the general meeting declaration and the method of collecting, safekeeping, and using donations. (7) Set the first joint meeting of directors and supervisors for 2:00 PM on the 28th. Forty-nine directors were elected on the spot: Xia Douyin, Ye Peng, Tu Weizeng, Chen Daxun, Lu Deze, Yang Zaichun, Chen Shi, Song Ruhai, Xie Chuheng, Wu Guozhen, Zhao Dianzhi, Li Shucheng, Cai Lisheng, Liu Shaoyan, Fang Benren, Zhao Zhongxuan, Xu Ziqing, Pu Xinya, Wu Xinming, Wang Yiling, Yu Zhonghan, Zhou Cangbai, Zhou Xingtang, He Hengfu, Chen Jingyu, Zhu Songshan, Yu Jusheng, Xiao Dengyun, Li Dezhai, Gao Bochang, Su Taiyu, Zhang Yikun, Yu Yuzhi, Cai Shuzhong, He Jingwu, Huang Yingzhong, Sun Yechao, Lou Botang, Chen Huaping, Qiu Ao, Hu Zhichu, Huang Shaokun, Li Huating, Liao Yaping, Liu Wensong, Li Kaichen, Ye Jiabi. Thirty-one supervisors were also elected: He Chengjun, Zhao YiKuan, Jin Jutang, Chen Wozu, Zhang Nanxian, Zhu Chuanjing, Wan Shengyang, Chen Hancun, Kong Geng, Li Fanyi, Wang Shijie, Jia Shiyi, Fan Xiji, Jiang Dingwen, Huang Wenzhi, Zeng Qingxi, Chen Xizeng, Zhou Weizhen, Zhou Shaoyuan, Ai Yuying, Zheng Huiwu, Xu Kejiu, Geng Bozhao, Hu Boxuan, Xia Ziwen, Xi Debing, Yu Rongqiao, Zhou Min, Yang Jinyu, He Wenbing, Xu Yuanquan. On the same day, airplanes flew around Wuhan, distributing leaflets. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM. (February 25)

Financial Crisis in Jinan 66

Two Banks Close Down

Deficit of More Than 800,000

Jinan Correspondence: Yijusheng Bank in this city suddenly closed down yesterday (23rd), with a market deficit of more than 300,000, causing a major panic in the financial community. It is currently under investigation. Only one night later, today (24th), Chengdehou Bank also closed down and declared bankruptcy, with an estimated deficit of more than 500,000. The news spread, shaking the entire city. Li Jianquan, the owner of Chengdehou Bank, was originally an unknown salt merchant. During Zhang Zongchang's time in Shandong in the 1920s, Li made a lot of profit by handling Xuan Yong bills and provincial bank bills, and thus became a seemingly wealthy merchant. Chengdehou Bank was established in his home (Xianxue Street). Li had extensive social connections and was lavish in his spending. Banks and silver firms considered him reliable due to his activities and were happy to deal with him. In fact, he did not have much capital. In addition, his salt business suffered many losses, and his extravagant spending gradually led to financial difficulties. Therefore, on the second day after Yijusheng Bank closed down, he declared bankruptcy. It is scheduled to be held at 3:00 PM tomorrow (25th) at his home to host a creditors' meeting to discuss bankruptcy and debt repayment methods. It is heard that his assets are very few, but the total deficit is 500,000 yuan. Those affected include five banks, thirteen silver firms, and ten individuals. Among those already identified are: Continental Bank 110,000 yuan, Shanghai Commercial Bank 60,000 yuan, China Industrial Bank 40,000 yuan, Zhonglu Bank 25,000 yuan, Shandong Commercial Bank 11,000 yuan, Xiejutai Bank 18,000 yuan, Deju 9,000 yuan, Jindaxiang 10,000 yuan, Dadetong 10,000 yuan, Deshengchang 8,000 yuan, and Yuanfengcheng 24,000 yuan.

After the collapse of Yangjusheng, the staff of its Lianhao Yijuzhan also fled. Qingdao Lianhao Yijucheng also collapsed on the same day. It is heard that Qingdao Yijucheng owes people 110,000 yuan and is owed 80,000 yuan. The bank issued a Shanghai exchange for 80,000 yuan. It is heard that after the incident, 50,000 yuan was deducted in Shanghai, but this has not yet been confirmed.

According to people in the financial community, native products, cotton yarn, and other companies suffered too many losses last year, and this year's market prices have plummeted again and again, with estimated total losses of more than 1 million yuan. If they cannot support it, the entire city's commerce will be at risk of collapse. (February 24)

[P Lu Province Establishes County Administration Construction Experimental Zone

Pilot Project in Zouping and Zou County

Director of the Experimental Department Concurrently Serves as Chief

Jinan Correspondence: Governor of Shandong Province Han Fuqu believes that improving internal affairs and promoting autonomy must start from rural areas, so he pays special attention to rural education and rural construction. He designated Zouping as a model county and hired rural education experts Liang Shuming, Liang Zhonghua, and others to come to Shandong. They established a Rural Construction Research Institute in Zouping, recruited several classes of students, and engaged in research and experimentation. For two years, they have achieved some results, but the scale is still small, not enough to accommodate many people, and sometimes restricted by laws and regulations, they cannot fully experiment. Therefore, they have now changed their approach, expanded it, and made it larger. At today's provincial government standing committee meeting, Han specially proposed the establishment of the Shandong Provincial County Administration Construction Research Institute Experimental Zone, which was passed as proposed. The content is as follows: A temporary report from the Secretariat stated that the Chairman has submitted a copy of the Shandong Provincial County Administration Construction Research Institute Experimental Zone Regulations, the original text is as follows: (1) These Regulations are formulated with reference to the Measures for Establishing County Administration Construction Experimental Zones in Various Counties of the Ministry of Interior Affairs (hereinafter referred to as the previous measures) passed by the Second National Internal Affairs Conference. (2) In accordance with the provisions of Articles 2, 3, and 8 of the previous measures, Zouping and Zou County are temporarily designated as the experimental zone. When necessary, the number of counties may be expanded. One zone chief officer is established to have overall responsibility for all administrative affairs within the experimental zone. (3) In accordance with the provisions of Article 7 of the previous measures, the county government and its affiliated agencies within the experimental zone may be reorganized and expanded as appropriate. (4) The organization of the zone chief officer's office shall be formulated separately in accordance with the provisions of Articles 8 and 10 of the previous measures. (5) In accordance with the provisions of Article 12 of the previous measures, the commanding and supervising offices of the zone chief officer's office and the county government, and the zone chief officer's office, the county government, and its affiliated agencies shall not communicate directly in writing. (6) In accordance with the provisions of Article 9 of the previous measures, the zone chief officer or county magistrate of the experimental zone shall concurrently serve as the director of the experimental department of the research institute, and shall be appointed by the provincial government upon presentation by the president of the research institute. (7) In accordance with the provisions of Article 13 of the previous measures, all administrative personnel within the experimental zone other than the zone chief officer and county magistrate shall be appointed by the president of the research institute. (8) In accordance with the provisions of Article 15 of the previous measures, if the implementation of central and provincial government laws and regulations within the experimental zone is considered difficult, (permission may be requested from the higher-level government for approval to make changes, and various individual laws and regulations may be formulated. (9) In accordance with the provisions of Article 16 of the previous measures, the scope of powers of the experimental zone is as follows: (1) Those matters that legally belong to the county; (2) Those undertakings that belong to the entire province but have an experimental nature; (3) Those matters specifically handled by the higher-level government. (10) The expenses and finances of each county within the experimental zone, in addition to the various expenses that should be handled in accordance with the laws and regulations of this province, shall be handled in accordance with the principles of the relevant articles of the previous measures. All local expenses may be budgeted separately and submitted to the provincial government for record. The detailed measures shall be formulated separately. (11) If there are any matters not covered in these Regulations, the County Administration Construction Research Institute shall submit them to the provincial government for amendment.]

Taiyuan Pacification Headquarters Promotes Reclamation 67

Selected 600 Qing of Fertile Wasteland in Western Suiyuan

Personnel from Military and Political Agencies Can Apply for Reclamation

Taiyuan Correspondence: The Taiyuan Pacification Headquarters, in order to promote reclamation in the northwest, has specially selected 600 qing of good fertile wasteland in western Suiyuan. Any staff member or military officer belonging to various agencies in Shanxi and Suiyuan who is willing to apply for reclamation can declare and process it. The Pacification Headquarters has also separately sent letters to the Shanxi and Suiyuan provincial governments, as well as various military agencies and troops in Shanxi and Suiyuan, with attached declaration forms, land reclamation measures, and a table of farming seasons in Suiyuan, ordering the subordinates to be informed and handled accordingly. After receiving the order, the Shanxi Provincial Government instructed all agencies to instruct their subordinates to handle it. The instruction document reads, [In accordance with] Taiyuan Pacification Headquarters, Reference Letter, Now, in order to encourage people to go to the northwest to engage in reclamation, 600 qing of good fertile wasteland have been specially selected in western Suiyuan. Any staff member or military officer belonging to various agencies in Shanxi and Suiyuan who is willing to apply for reclamation should follow the attached land reclamation measures and submit a declaration to this headquarters by the end of February for processing. In addition to notifying various military agencies and troops, a separate letter is sent to the Suiyuan Provincial Government accordingly, hoping that you will investigate and instruct the personnel of your affiliated agencies to be informed and handled accordingly, etc., attached are the original documents of the land reclamation measures, etc. Upon receiving this, in addition to submitting a reply and sending separate letters accordingly, we hereby urgently send the original documents to your office for investigation and instruction to the personnel of your affiliated agencies to be informed and handled accordingly]. As for the land reclamation measures, (1) Those who are willing to reclaim wasteland in Suiyuan shall submit a declaration to the Taiyuan Pacification Headquarters and the Baotou Reclamation Supervision Office, respectively. (2) The declaration period is from January 15 of this year to the end of February of this year. (3) After the deadline, the Pacification Headquarters and the Reclamation Supervision Office will separately convene the land reclamation households to elect responsible personnel to carry out land reclamation and prepare for all matters. (4) The land reclamation procedure shall be handled in accordance with the regulations of the Suiyuan Reclamation Bureau. The land price shall be paid in installments as stipulated. (5) Each person shall not reclaim more than 20 qing of land, but this is not applicable to social welfare organizations recognized by the government. (6) Those who reclaim land may operate individually, in which case the individual shall register. If they wish to operate in partnership, the partners shall jointly register. If they wish to organize a company to operate, the company shall be established in accordance with the company regulations, and the company shall register. This shall be indicated in the declaration form. (7) When necessary, those who reclaim land may declare to the Suiyuan Reclamation Supervision Office for guidance or assistance. (8) The wasteland released for reclamation is located in the Houtao area of Suiyuan. (9) The land price is divided into several grades according to the quality of the land, and the price per qing is approximately 8 yuan.

Demonstrating the Evolution of the Rule of Law in China in Recent Years

Since Ju Zheng took over as the President of the Supreme Court, he has actively reorganized it. The content of each chart and graph is rich in science and artistry, and it demonstrates the evolution of the rule of law in China in recent years, which is truly a valuable work. Wuxi

New Weights and Measures are Successfully Implemented

Because the local Nandhuo Industry Association was ordered to switch to the municipal scale on March 1, it convened a general meeting of all members on the afternoon of the previous day (25th). Chairman Miao Dongchen reported first, briefly saying that the goods from Shanghai in our industry have all switched to the new scale, but the sales in this county still use the old scale, which has a huge loss. We should quickly switch to the municipal scale in accordance with the order. It was decided that the switch would be implemented on March 1, and all old scales would be handed over to the association for safekeeping. The door-to-door prices would be reduced uniformly, and a list of prices would be recorded separately and sent to each store, which must not be increased or decreased without authorization, so as to ensure fairness. The meeting adjourned after the discussion. The sauce and wine industries will also use measuring instruments from April 1. Inspectors Tang Fuxuan and Qin Hebing have been inspecting the clothing industry for days and found more than 100 old rulers, which were taken back to the county government and confiscated uniformly.

Nantong, Tong, Abolishes Fishing Protection Team

The River North Tong's Fisheries Administration's protection team was abolished by order of the Ministry of Industry. The coastal protection facilities will be handled by the Fisheries Improvement Association.

Jiaxing Four-County Highway Conference Minutes

Jiaxing, Jiashan, Pinghu, and Haiyan counties convened a meeting at the Jiaxing County Government on the 25th to discuss the construction of highways. The items for discussion are as follows: The road lines will be built in two phases. The first phase will be at the end of the 22nd year, and the road lines to be built are: (A) Pinghu to Jiashan, (B) Jiashan to Xitang, (C) Xinfeng to Xinhua Shendang. The second phase will be at the end of the 23rd year, and the road lines to be built are: (A) Shendang to Ganpu, (B) Xinhua to Jiashan, (C) Haiyan to Tanghua, (D) Zhapu to Pinghu. The cost is tentatively set at 400,000 yuan, which will be borne by the province and the counties. The 200,000 yuan for the four counties is divided into five shares, and Jiaxing gets two shares, and should pay 80,000 yuan. The money will be allocated from the sale of the city bricks and surplus land from the Shiqiu city wall. If the four counties have difficulty raising funds, they may mortgage the property rights of the entire road to the financial community for cash, or the Highway Bureau may issue stocks and use the revenue of the entire road as a mortgage.

Qingjiang, Qingzhen Small Boats Resume Long Trips

The small boats of the Qingjiang and Qingzhen companies on the inner river have not been running long trips since the Mapengwan blocked the construction of a river dam. Until the dam was released last winter, the river water froze again, so even short trips were stopped. Now that the river water is melting and the water is increasing, two upstream long trips have arrived in the past two days, one is the Chunxian steamboat of the Fuyun Company and the Fuqing tugboat, and the other is the Guangjiang steamboat of the Zhentong Company and the Qingjiang tugboat. Therefore, the various boat companies here have also opened downstream trips from (22nd) onwards, directly reaching Zhenjiang, restoring the old routes before the dam was built.

Local News

University Professors' Conference Discusses Ways to Cope with National Crisis 69

Xiong Xiling and Wang Renzhi Report on the Situation in North China

All Advocate for Chairman Chiang to Go North to Resist the Enemy

The Shanghai University Professors' Association, in response to the start of the Battle of Rehe, convened a general meeting yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM at the China Society on Weihaiwei Road. More than 20 people attended, including Wang Zaoshi, Zhu Qinglai, Zuo Shunsheng, Shen Hengshan, Xie Xunchu, Wu Zelin, Yang Weiyu, Peng Jiuying, and Pan Dakui. Mr. Xiong Bing-san and Mr. Huang Renzhi were invited to report on the situation in North China, discuss countermeasures, and re-elect directors. Details are recorded below:

Xiong Xiling's Report

The meeting began at 3:00 PM, chaired by Wang Zaoshi. He first reported that representatives of professors from universities in Peiping and Tianjin had come south, but had not yet arrived in Shanghai because negotiations in Beijing were not yet complete. Mr. Xiong Bing-san arrived in Shanghai yesterday from Peiping, and the association respectfully invited him to report on the situation in North China. Mr. Xiong stood up and reported that the situation in Rehe was precarious, surrounded by mountains, commanding a high position. Its importance was even greater than that of Peiping and Tianjin. Currently, the battlefields, except for Kailu, which is a plain, are all in towering mountains and steep ridges, such as Lingyuan, Beipiao, and Chaoyangsi, which are easy to defend and difficult to attack. Even Kailu requires traversing sixty li of mountain roads, all narrow paths, truly a situation where "one man guards the pass, and ten thousand cannot pass." Within Rehe, there are more than hundreds of thousands of local militia, with nearly two hundred thousand rifles. The local customs are robust, as it was the imperial hunting ground during the Qing Dynasty, and the residents are accustomed to martial arts. When I (Xiong referring to himself) served as the Governor of Rehe, I trained more than one hundred thousand local militia. Later, when the Feng army was defeated and withdrew from the pass, two divisions of troops were disarmed by the Rehe militia. Therefore, their strength is quite considerable. It will not be easy for the Japanese to invade this area. However, Rehe Province has always been poor. In the past, the central government assisted with hundreds of thousands [of dollars] annually. When Zhang Zuolin became the Grand Marshal, he stopped the subsidies. Subsequently, the local authorities took everything from the people. When Tang Yulin governed the province, the land tax increased to four yuan per mu, and the people's livelihood became difficult. Later, through my efforts and those of General Zhu Ziqiao, we vigorously negotiated with the central government and North China authorities for subsidies, so that Rehe Province could stop collecting the land tax. Fortunately, it was successful, and the people's strength was somewhat relieved. The military deployment is also in place, and the command of the formal army and the volunteer army is also moving towards unification. However, Rehe is barren and the people are poor. In recent months, the volunteer armies from the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang have gathered on the Rehe border, and there is a danger of food shortages. It is hoped that assistance can be provided. The morale of the lower-ranking officers and soldiers in North China is very high. The troops set out as soon as they receive orders, without demanding any expenses for departure. The soldiers expressed that in the current war of resistance against Japan, people from all walks of life come to comfort them, showing the great kindness of the Chinese people. How can we not fight desperately? He also stated that although our army does not have airplanes and artillery, the Japanese cannot occupy our land solely relying on airplanes and artillery. They must use infantry or cavalry to charge before they can occupy our positions. We must vow to hold on to the death, never give up our positions, and not allow the Japanese invaders to cross the Lei Pool one step. The battle of Rehe and eastern Hebei is related to the survival of our country. I hope the whole country will rise up to help, fully supply food and military supplies, and especially hope that Chairman Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission will personally go north to supervise the army. Then the victory is in our grasp, etc.

Huang Renzhi's Report

Next, Huang Renzhi, the representative of the Shanghai Local Association who went north, reported that since the September 18th Incident, he had gone north twice, in July of last year and January of this year. His impression was that there were three points: (1) lack of unified command at the front; (2) lack of organization at the rear; (3) lack of financial resources. This month, he and representatives of the Local Association, Mu Ouchou, Hu Yunzhuang, Yang Zhixiong, etc., went north again. Fortunately, Dean Song also arrived in Peiping around the same time. The above three shortcomings began to be addressed one by one, and considerable measures were taken. If Rehe can hold for three months, then the "green screen" will rise, and the Japanese, even with airplanes and other new weapons, will have no way to use their skills. For the sake of reliable security in North China, and for the future of the entire country, I hope that Chairman Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission can personally go north to supervise the army.

Passage of Various Resolutions

After the reports by Xiong and Huang, discussions began on countermeasures. Peng Wenyin, Xie Xunchu, Pan Dakui, Zuo Shunsheng, Zhu Qinglai, Zheng Xi, Gu, and others spoke and debated one after another. Then, the following resolutions were passed: (1) Resolution to reward and comfort the frontline soldiers. A: Send a telegram to the frontline to encourage the soldiers. B: Invite Mr. Shen Junru to represent the association and go north to comfort the troops. (2) Send a telegram to the Military Affairs Commission, requesting Chairman Chiang to personally go north to supervise the army. (3) Initiate a fundraising campaign. The procedures and methods will be determined and implemented by the board of directors. (4) Five principles of policy toward Japan were contributed to the government and passed: A: Declare war on Japan. B: Recall the ambassador to Japan and declare a severance of diplomatic relations. C: Order a total political, economic, and military mobilization of the country. D: Launch a counterattack on the three northeastern provinces and Japanese concessions. E: Organize a national volunteer army to conduct guerrilla warfare, and prepare the national combat teams for a long-term war. The five domestic items will be temporarily reserved.

Election of New Directors

After the discussion, the directors were elected by ballot. Yang Weiyu and Zhu Qinglai counted the votes. Wang Zaoshi, Shen Hengshan, Zhu Qinglai, Zuo Shunsheng, Xie Xunchu, Wu Zelin, Zhang Yousan, Zheng Xigu, Jin Tongyin, Chen XuanShan, Yang Weiyu and other eleven people were elected as directors. Peng Wenyin, Pan Dakui, Xie Chengping, Zhang Peijun, Yu Naichuan, and other five people were elected as alternate directors. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Shanghai General Labor Union Issues Letter to Workers Nationwide 70

Three Main Points

Save on Food and Clothing to Fully Support Military Supplies

Vigorously Resist Goods and Intensify Anti-Japanese Work

Strive for Production and Implement Labor-Management Cooperation

According to the Dagong News Agency, the Shanghai General Labor Union, in view of the outbreak of the Rehe War and the serious situation, yesterday issued a letter to workers nationwide, stating that the brutal Japanese, disregarding justice and betraying good faith, took advantage of our great flood to seize the three northeastern provinces with lightning speed, and created a puppet organization. In order to respect the League of Nations Covenant and maintain peace in East Asia, we have not hesitated to endure humiliation and repeatedly make concessions. However, the Japanese bandits, like wild boars and long snakes, have endlessly nibbled away at our territory. Recently, after capturing Yuguan, they mobilized a large army to launch a general offensive against Rehe, attempting to fulfill their delusion of swallowing the Northeast and destroying China. Their ferocity and violence have reached their extreme, and their arrogance has reached its limit. Our North China generals, unable to bear it any longer, deeply understand that at this critical moment, there is no way to survive without fighting and no way to save ourselves without sacrificing ourselves. Therefore, they resolutely and decisively sent a telegram, expressing their determination to resist violence and defend the country to the death. Now that the war has broken out, Japan is also tilting its national strength to invade us. The situation is tense and has reached the most serious stage. We must unite as one, exert our efforts to resist the enemy, and save the country from danger and protect the national lineage. The association dares to express its sincere hope and briefly list a few things to tell our most beloved workers nationwide: (1) We should save on food and clothing and do our best to support [军需] the war effort. Defending the homeland and resisting the enemy is the duty of soldiers. Saving on food and clothing, donating money and grain is the obligation of the people. Now that the war has begun, the soldiers at the front have bravely resisted violence and vowed to resist to the death, and the volunteer armies in various places are even more persevering and fighting bloody battles. We, the people in the rear, should prepare grain and supplies, donate money and silk, and fully support them to boost morale and express the people's will. Our national workers have always had extremely ardent patriotic emotions. They should not shirk their responsibility, quickly rise up to provide assistance, so that military strength is strong and morale is high, and it can be expected that the enemy will be wiped out. (2) We should vigorously resist Japanese goods and intensify the anti-Japanese movement. Japan, as a small and poor country, relies on the development of industry and commerce and the sales of inferior goods to us to achieve its current wealth and strength and cultivate its aggressive violence. We must vigorously boycott Japanese goods to strike at its economic lifeline. This task is especially our revolutionary workers' unshirkable responsibility. We deeply hope that workers nationwide will unite, intensify anti-Japanese work, and adopt strict and effective means to carry out an organized boycott movement. Then the Japanese financial stagnation, economic collapse, its desire to engage in further militarism, I am afraid, is also impossible. (3) We should unite and work together to overcome national difficulties. The matter is urgent, the disaster is approaching, the national crisis is serious, and it has reached the final stage. We must gather the entire strength of the country to cope with this critical situation. In addition to doing their best to support the anti-Japanese soldiers and vigorously boycott Japanese goods, the national workers must unite as one, strive to increase production on the one hand, and strive to coordinate labor and management on the other, help each other with sincerity, and work together to resist the enemy. Then, relieving difficulties and saving the country can be expected. The association is not talented, but dares to encourage all workers nationwide.

The Work and Organization of the Northeastern Association 73

Recruitment of Members in Two Weeks

Regular Board Meeting Tomorrow

The Northeastern Association is a successor organization for helping and educating those in the Northeast. Its purpose is to assist the soldiers fighting in the Northeast, investigate the current and past conditions of the three northeastern provinces, study the solution to the Northeast issue, and unite various national organizations to jointly assist in exerting the entire nation's perseverance and determination to seek a solution to the Northeast issue. At the beginning of its establishment, the founders, Wu Tiecheng, Shi Liangcai, and others, clearly declared its purpose. The entire board of directors of the association jointly declared the other day, detailing the purpose of the establishment and the heavy responsibility it bears, in order to awaken the people of the country to unite from top to bottom and carry out the general mobilization of the entire nation to achieve its purpose. A reporter from the Central News Agency, in order to understand the current status of the association's planning and organization, specifically went to the association's executive director, Zang Qifang, and received a detailed answer as follows:

Two Important Tasks

Zang told the reporter, the purpose of the establishment of the Northeastern Association has been described in detail in the declaration published the other day, and the people of the country should have understood it. What we are planning now is the work plan. The most important things are two points: (1) How to enable the volunteer army in the Northeast to fight together with the national army under unified leadership. (2) To investigate the recent situation in the three northeastern provinces and the internal workings of the puppet organization and Japan in order to study the coping strategies. After Ma Zhanshan, Feng Zhanhai, Ding Chao, Li Du and others successively went abroad last year, the spirit of the Northeast Volunteer Army seemed to have declined. However, in reality, there are still no less than 200,000 people in the Northeast who are waiting for orders. However, due to the lack of leadership or the cut-off of supplies, they are hiding in the deep mountains, waiting for opportunities. Moreover, due to the strict investigation by the Japanese military, domestic news cannot be conveyed there. Therefore, although they are ready, they do not yet know that the time to kill the enemy and serve the country has matured. Now the war on the Rehe border has broken out, so it is a good opportunity for the volunteer army to rise up in response to attack from the rear. If the national army in Rehe Province can maintain for three months, then the crushing defeat of Japan should be within expectation. Even if Rehe Province unfortunately falls, the association's support for the volunteer army will not be reduced at all. The effectiveness of the volunteer army fighting within its interior is actually greater than sending troops to recover lost land. Therefore, the association must provide leadership and assistance on the one hand, and transmit all kinds of news to that place on the other hand, so that they can rise up in time.

Recruitment of Members in Two Weeks

Continuing to talk about the recruitment of members, Zang said that the planning of the association will be completed in about two weeks. Therefore, the recruitment period is not too far away. The association is a large group for saving the Northeast and solving the Northeast issue, so we hope that all compatriots nationwide will be members. Mayor Wu once said that the Northeast issue must be deeply imprinted in the minds of compatriots nationwide and alerted at any time and place, that even after the Northeast is recovered, we must not forget the great responsibility of the Northeast's construction. But human life is limited, and the Northeast issue may not be resolved in a short period of time. Therefore, if the Northeastern Association exists, even if it is passed down to our children and grandchildren, it will not forget the Northeast. As for its organization, it must be popularized throughout the country, and branch associations will be established for members in various places. Its internal organization will add several special committees as needed. The Foreign Affairs Committee, which was decided by the last board of directors, is already underway and will conduct detailed investigations and studies on the international issues of the Northeast in the future to contribute to government references. Other committees such as the Economic Committee and the Advisory Committee will also be established in order to study various specialized issues.

Regular Board Meeting Tomorrow

Zang said at the end that the association has scheduled the first regular board meeting for tomorrow (Monday) at 4:30 pm at the Municipal Government to discuss all the proceedings. As for the venue, it was originally intended to be attached to the China Aviation Association, but now because the association's houses are not enough to use, it has been relocated separately and will be moved into the office after repairs.

According to the Central News Agency, the Swiss Consul in Shanghai, Tan Like, was ordered by the Swiss government last winter to be promoted to the position of Chargé d'Affaires in Japan. According to sources from the Swiss Consulate in Shanghai, Mr. Tan Like left Shanghai a few days ago to take up his new position as Chargé d'Affaires in Japan. As for the successor, he has not yet arrived in Shanghai, and all the duties of the Consul are temporarily handled by the Consul General. Mr. Tan has been in Shanghai for many years and has served as the Acting Consul General for a long time. He has an extraordinary admiration for Chinese culture and philosophy. Before leaving, Mr. Tan agreed to the reporter's request to convey the Chinese people's love of peace and determination to maintain justice to the government and people of his country.

Jin Baoguang Appointed as Management Engineer of Shanghai Wireless Radio Station 77

Officially Taking Over on March 1st

The Management Engineer of the Shanghai Wireless Radio Station of the Ministry of Communications will be sent to England at the end of this month to investigate the China-UK telecommunications matters. Yan Renguang, the Director of the Department of Electrical Administration of the Ministry of Communications, appointed Jin Baoguang, a technician of the Ministry, to succeed him. After graduating from Jiaotong University, Jin was appointed as an engineer of the Shanghai Wireless Radio Station by the Ministry of Communications, and was later transferred to Wuhu, Tianjin, Qingdao and other wireless stations as an engineer. Recently, he was transferred to the Ministry to serve as a technician and achieved remarkable results. He is trusted by the previous communications authorities and is greatly loved by the staff of each radio station. He is now promoted to the Management Engineer of the Shanghai Wireless Radio Station by the Ministry's order. Mr. Jin came to Shanghai from Beijing yesterday and is scheduled to officially take over on March 1st.
