Economic Special Issue No. 12 Published Every Monday

Reflections After the Fixation of the Foreign Cent 153

—Pan Shihao

Since March 1st, the Shanghai Monetary Association has fixed the foreign cent at 7 qian 15 li, establishing a permanent exchange rate between silver dollars and silver taels. All currency market prices, such as small silver dollars, will henceforth use silver dollars as the standard for expressing market prices, and all account calculations will be based on silver dollars as the unit. Silver dollars have thus taken the inherent position of silver taels and replaced them. The date of implementation is only two days away (March 1st). Looking back at the past and contemplating the future, one cannot remain silent.

In fact, China originally had no so-called "foreign cent." Since 1497, the Mexican silver dollar has been popular and widely circulated from the states of North America to the Philippines and the ports of China. Thus, in Ningbo, Xiamen, Shanghai, and other places, in addition to the existing silver taels, the British silver dollar was used as a unit of account (because of the eagle on the coin, it was commonly called the eagle dollar, abbreviated as the British dollar). The foreign cent was created by the fluctuation of the exchange rate between the two. At that time, the influence of the eagle dollar was less than that of silver taels. The general public regarded silver taels as the national treasure and eagle dollars as foreign currency. All official and commercial accounting was based on silver taels as the principal currency. Therefore, the exchange rate between the two was expressed in foreign cents. In other words, silver taels were the principal currency, and foreign silver dollars were subsidiary currency. This was the period of origin for the foreign cent.

In the thirteenth year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty [1887], the Guangdong Governor Zhang Zhidong was granted permission to mint domestic silver dollars to resist foreign silver dollars. The provinces of Guangdong, Hubei, Hunan, Zhili, Anhui, Zhejiang, Fengtian, Jilin, Fujian, Yunnan, Shandong, and Henan successively opened mints, totaling seventeen silver dollar bureaus. Because the coin designs were largely similar but slightly different, and the quality could not be consistent, discrimination arose during transactions. Thus, the types of silver dollars increased, and the market prices of foreign cents became more mixed. Taking Shanghai as an example, British dollars already had their own foreign cent, and dragon dollars such as those from Jiangnan, Hubei, Guangdong, and Fengtian each had their own foreign cent as well. Those that did not have official market prices were either traded by analogy or used with a discount, resulting in chaos and complexity, all the negative phenomena of a "miscellaneous currency system." Therefore, although the circulation volume of silver dollars increased daily and the actual transactions of silver taels gradually decreased, silver dollars still did not shed their status as subsidiary currency, and silver taels were indeed able to maintain their qualification as the primary currency. This was the period of chaos for the foreign cent. In the third year of the Republic [1914], the Tianjin General Mint, according to the National Currency Regulations, began minting new silver coins with Yuan Shikai's image. The Jiangnan Mint followed suit. The design and quality were fairly uniform, and the volume of circulation gradually increased. Old-style silver dollars were successively withdrawn and reminted, and the chaotic state of currency in the market gradually decreased. In April and August, the Shanghai Sino-Foreign Two Banks and the Money Trade Association negotiated that, in addition to British dollars, new coins, and Jiangnan, Hubei, Guangdong, and Qing silver coins, which would still be quoted separately, all other kinds of dragon dollars could be exchanged for new coins at a rate fixed by the banks, without separate quotations. This was gradually followed by other ports, and the foreign cent gradually became unified. This was the period when various kinds of foreign cents gradually disappeared.

After Mexico adopted the gold exchange standard, the minting of eagle dollars ceased, and the Yuan Shikai silver dollars were minted in increasing numbers each year. Although its quality and foreign cent were different from those of the eagle dollar, the general public in society mostly counted the number of coins and did not bother to calculate their weight and quality in detail. Thus, Gresham's Law occurred, and the stock of British dollars dwindled daily. Foreign banks could no longer specialize in eagle dollars for collection, remittance, and exchange. In June of the eighth year of the Republic [1919], Shanghai's local silver and money industries negotiated with foreign banks to abolish the eagle dollar foreign cent market and universally use new coins. Subsequently, the silver dollar market only quoted one type of new coin, the Yuan Shikai coin. All coins from Jiangnan, Hubei, and Guangdong were universally used, and various other domestic silver dollars with excessively low weight and quality were successively withdrawn and reminted. The public found this convenient, and other ports responded one after another. The foreign cent was thus unified from this point onward. After the establishment of the National Government, when the Sun Yat-sen silver dollar came into existence, the unification of the foreign cent remained unimpeded. This was the period of unification of the foreign cent. However, silver taels always retained their qualification as the principal currency in calculations. Whoever used silver dollars for accounting still had to fictitiously set an "immobile foreign cent" as the unit and reconcile it with the daily opening foreign cent. In reality, silver dollars were still just a type of subsidiary currency.

Now, the Shanghai monetary industry has decided to fix the foreign cent. Fixing the foreign cent can be said to be abolishing the market price of silver dollars. It can also be said to be abolishing the foreign cent. This is truly the initial success of the movement to abolish taels and use dollars, and a major change in the financial world for decades. It can be divided into an era in financial and economic history, and I cannot help but feel deeply about this. (I) Reflections on the Monetary System: Currency is a medium of exchange, and its own price should not change, just like weights and measures, which are used to weigh all things. Its own standard should remain unchanged. Only when it is unchanged can it be a guideline for transactions and a medium of exchange. This is the general meaning of monetary theory. Since China began minting silver dollars in the Qing Dynasty, the state has legislated for it to be the main currency for a long time. However, in reality, silver dollars had a market-based foreign cent, and its own value had to be weighed against silver taels. How could it have the qualification of a flat currency, let alone be the main currency? It was just a kind of subsidiary currency. Therefore, the proposal to abolish taels and use dollars has been around for decades, and the theory of reforming the monetary system has been voluminous. The currency actually transacted, silver dollars, was used far more than silver taels, but silver dollars ultimately failed to take the place of silver taels and complete their qualification as the primary currency. This is all because of this. If silver dollars, which have long been designated as the national currency, have not obtained their qualification as currency, then discussions on the monetary standard and studies on currency reform are not the most important topics at present. In other words, only by abolishing taels and using dollars can we begin to talk about the monetary system. Therefore, the decision of the Shanghai money industry to use silver dollars as the main currency is worthy of public praise. The term "silver dollars as the main currency" may not be understood by the general public, but in fact, since the foreign cent has been abolished implicitly, its own price has not changed, and it can be directly and easily used as a unit of currency for accounting. In addition, factors such as unlimited legal tender and free minting have already been clearly stipulated in the law. The qualification of silver dollars as the main currency has already been fully established. On the other hand, silver taels, in the near future, seem to have become a kind of lame standard with silver dollars. In fact, once the qualification of silver dollars as the main currency is established, silver taels will lose their basis for weighing all currencies, and there is no doubt that they will be eliminated as a kind of commodity-like silver. However, this theory may still be too optimistic. Why do I say this? Since the foreign cent entered the country with British dollars, it has undergone several changes before finally reaching the recent decision by the money industry to fix it. The reason for this can be said to be due to the abolition of the tael and the use of the dollar movement in the government and the public, and it can also be said to be due to the fact that silver dollars in society have become more uniform. Only when silver dollars have become more uniform can their use be convenient and the foreign cent can be single and stable. In recent months, the theory that the government will mint new coins has been widely rumored, but the weight and quality of these coins are unknown. If there are differences between these coins and the current coins, will the foreign cent still be single and stable? Will silver dollars still be able to maintain their uniform state? If their uniform state cannot be maintained, then problems will arise between silver dollars themselves. Can we prevent the silver tael system from reviving in a disguised form? This is the first reason why it is difficult to be optimistic. The second reason is that I have often argued that there are several reasons for the obstacles to the abolition of the tael and the use of the dollar, which are related to the system of taels and dollars themselves. In other words, although taels are fictitious currencies, they retain the decimal system that has existed for a very long time. There is no lack of convenience in accounting and calculation. Although silver dollars are national currencies, their so-called auxiliary currencies, such as dimes and copper coins, have daily market prices and do not have the qualification of currency. Because people are used to them and the distinction between whole and miscellaneous is clear, it is not easy for dollars to rise. Now that the foreign cent is fixed, silver taels are equivalent to ceasing. However, the silver dollar's own system has not yet been established. In fact, the National Currency Regulations only mention silver dollars. All auxiliary currencies can be said to be not yet established. How can we plan for convenience in use? This is another reason why it is difficult to be optimistic.

(II) Reflections on the Strength of the Monetary Industry: The monetary industry has a long history. Foreigners call them Native Banks. Those who praise them praise their simplicity and stability, while those who criticize them see them as conservative and calculating. In fact, conservatism forms the virtue of simplicity and stability, and caution is not to be criticized in business. Moreover, in terms of their conservatism, they are indeed conservative. In terms of their evolution, there is indeed something to be praised. Therefore, they have always occupied a large amount of influence in China's financial world. For example, in the matter of the foreign cent, the abolition of the market price of miscellaneous dragon dollars and the standardization of the market price of British dragon dollars could not have been achieved without their help. Industry insiders have always said that the decision on the market price of the foreign cent is in the hands of the monetary industry. In addition to a few famous banks, foreigners and foreign banks trust the monetary industry more than banks. There is some truth to this. The decision of the Shanghai monetary industry to fix the foreign cent will have far-reaching effects. Can the industry insiders make good use of this potential influence to help the improvement of the monetary and financial system? Or will they be complacent and be content to be passively pushed forward? Or will they even create obstacles to hinder the progress of all parties? This is probably not a question of system, but a question of people.

The one-two-five issue and the two-five issue of the foreign cent are what people in the monetary industry see as calculating, but the industry insiders can resolutely cancel them. Now that the foreign cent is fixed, the silver tael exchange rate has risen again. In the near future, silver taels should still be used. It is hoped that the industry insiders can carry out the original intention of canceling the buckle and not seek undue profits in the calculation. You must know that the cancellation of the buckle and the fixation of the price of the foreign cent in recent months and the abolition of the silver tael standard system are not so much an opportunity to be missed as a recognition that they have fallen behind. Instead of saying that they are active, it is better to see them as being passive.

Wartime Economy for Current Issues 154

—Mao Zhenchu

The Rehe War, concerning the life and death of China, has finally been initiated by ambitious and violent Japan! The importance of this war is such that we should mobilize all of China's manpower, financial resources, and material resources to cope with this war. At the front, of course, is where [manpower] is most concentrated, using flesh and blood to attack the enemy. At the rear, [financial resources] and [material resources] should be concentrated to cope with changes in the environment. In view of the facts of past world wars, I believe that it is necessary to strictly implement wartime economic organizations.

During the World War from 1914 to 1918, the entire economic organizations of all countries, including England, France, Germany, Austria, Russia, and Italy, were involved in the whirlpool of war. All of them temporarily implemented all economic policies to cope with this extraordinary state. At the beginning of the outbreak of the war in England, the economy immediately shook completely, the exchange closed, foreign exchange was cut off, financial panic, and industrial unrest. Therefore, the government immediately promulgated the order to extend the bank holiday and the suspension of debt payment, and transferred all railways, insurance, and other businesses to state-owned. On August 6, 1914, it also implemented the Currency and Bank Note Act, and at the same time abolished the previously promulgated banking regulations to restrict the issuance of banknotes by various banks. The French government, like the British government, initially ordered the postponement of the performance of contracts on the exchange, and then promulgated the debt relief order. In order to implement the relief of the financial difficulties and raise the expenses of the army's mobilization, it could only use the power of the central bank to control finances. However, as the scope of the war gradually expanded, relying on the power of the central bank alone was useless. At the end of August 1914, the cabinet was reorganized, and Li Bo's wartime financial policy was finally decided. The foundation of this policy was to issue inconvertible banknotes to serve as war expenses. Later, because these banknotes flooded the country, it used a kind of government long-term bonds to recover them, and at the same time increased taxes to overcome the difficulties of spending. Germany was relatively prepared in advance. In 1913 (the year before the war), it was actively preparing for war, expanding the army and navy as much as possible. Therefore, at that time, on the one hand, it issued huge special military bonds, and on the other hand, it levied a huge direct property tax of 500 million yuan. Therefore, in fact, after the war began, it no longer levied anything from the people. After the war started, the first to suffer a direct impact was of course the industry, trade, and shipping industries. Due to the impact of trade and shipping, food and raw materials that had always been supplied from foreign countries felt a lack at the same time, which caused difficulties for the manufacturing industries concerned, especially the manufacturing difficulties of military supplies. Therefore, the Raw Materials Bureau was established, and the German Electrical Association was established, so that all German industrial groups were of one heart and one mind for the general mobilization of the war for a month. The most important position in Germany's wartime economy was the food problem. Although the government tried all kinds of measures, such as restricting the excessive rise in grain prices, setting price limits, stipulating that wheat bread and rye wheat and potatoes should be used as military bread, establishing wartime grain agencies, and all grain supplies were controlled by the government under the monopoly system, and compulsory issuance of bread coupons was distributed to the people, etc., in the end, due to being trapped by the blockade of the Allied Powers, the food supply was on the verge of exhaustion. Other Allied countries, such as Japan and the United States, were also in a state of extreme chaos, and the wild drop in currency prices affected anywhere in the world.

Therefore, when a wide-ranging war started in Germany, everything was abnormal. Even if Germany had prepared before the war, it still had to panic to such an extent, let alone without preparation before the war! Now, we and the enemy have actually reached a state of war, just lacking a formal declaration of war. In such a critical autumn, how can there be no organization in the economy? According to my opinion, the financial aspect has the precedent of the European War to refer to, and the government should refer to the domestic people's livelihood and industry to formulate a suitable method to implement it. One [manpower] aspect focuses on military [censored] people, and let the military authorities plan it. The most uncertain thing is probably still in the [material resources] aspect. Usually, most of our daily necessities are supplied by foreign countries. If we are in the same situation as Germany, being blockaded by the enemy, wouldn't we be in the same desperate situation as Germany? It is good that foreign countries are now having excess production. We may wish to take advantage of this and purchase a large amount of military, daily, and necessary goods from overseas before the sea ports are blockaded (of course, this refers to those that are not available or not many in domestic goods) to prepare for a protracted war. Some people say that China had a bumper harvest last year, and there is no [censored] problem in terms of food. In fact, this observation is also wrong. Originally, last year's excess of grain was an abnormal rather than a normal situation. According to the statistics of imported foreign rice over the years, as well as the vast area of bandit areas, disaster areas, and barren areas in Hubei and other provinces, and the lack of food in Fujian, Guangdong, and other provinces, if we do not try to store grain widely, we will definitely not be able to fight for a long time! We believe that it is necessary in fact to use surplus agricultural products such as foreign wheat to prepare for food. In addition, we should also use the efforts of the people to set up various cooperative organizations. Such as investigation agencies, transportation agencies, requisition agencies, distribution agencies, etc., everything is concentrated to adapt to the special economic situation of this war, so that the military can have a solid backing.

Women and Economics in China 155

— Tang Mozeng

(1) The Position of Women in Past and Present Economic Organizations

When studying the past and present economic progress of China, commentators often emphasize the creation of men and overlook the contributions of women. In fact, in past economic history, women occupied an important position. In modern economic organizations, much relies on the assistance of women, and speculating on future situations, the mission borne by women is even more significant and cannot be ignored. Now, let us first talk about the past. Our country has been an agricultural country since ancient times, and the development of agriculture has relied on the division of labor between men and women. Ancient books often contain records of [men plowing and women weaving]. It is also said: [If one man does not plow, some will be hungry; if one woman does not weave, some will be cold.] The chapter on labor and leisure by Jing Jiang in the "Guoyu" (Discourses of the States) is especially passed down as a beautiful story by later generations, showing that the labor of women is also a driving force for promoting economic organization and cannot be ignored. In the process of economic evolution in Western countries, women's contributions were also very important. In the Greek and Roman eras, men's lives were mostly spent in warfare, so agricultural affairs were mostly undertaken by women. After the Industrial Revolution, the method of production changed drastically, and women were also very active in the industrial world. Our country also has this situation. In terms of material things, there are a large number of female workers in cities, all working in factories. According to surveys, the current number of female workers in our country accounts for 30% to 40% of the total number of employees, which is not a small number. In terms of service and professional occupations, the number of women serving in the business world in our country is gradually increasing (such as in banks and companies). As for those who have contributed in the arts, such as in music, fine arts, and literature, there are all outstanding talents. It is predicted that in the future, women in our country will leap to the same position as men in society, working together to seek the progress of the social economy. This is not an impossible thing.

(2) Women as Important Members in Today's Transformation of China's Economic Society

Since Chinese women have jointly created this existing economic society with men in the past, modern women should continue the enterprising spirit of their predecessors and strive to transform today's economic organization. This can be discussed in several points:

(1) Regarding Consumers

Commentators believe that the economic crisis in China today is due to the failure of consumption to adapt to production. With the production forms of the 16th and 17th centuries, and the consumption of the 20th century, the two sides lose their balance, and the national livelihood is inevitably on the verge of bankruptcy. This statement is very insightful. Frugality is a virtue and has always been a strength of our nation. In the past decade or so, social customs have become increasingly extravagant. Unnecessary waste among residents in rural areas is minimal, but in cities, the habit of luxury has become common. If this continues, the future is greatly worrying. Consumption can be divided into productive consumption and non-productive consumption. The advantages and disadvantages between them are far apart. For example, using production methods in farms and setting up machinery, although it is consumption, it is beneficial and harmless. Furthermore, if we want to seek knowledge and set up schools, it is also productive consumption. As for purchasing luxury goods to expand the market for foreign goods, it is not only useless to society but also harmful. It is non-productive consumption. The former should be promoted in our country, and the latter is tantamount to a suicidal policy and must be distinguished.

(2) Regarding Producers

Today, it seems that women in our country have not thoroughly studied how to use capital. There are many speculators and few investors. Women in rural areas only know how to hoard, and goods are abandoned on the ground. This is obviously a mistake. Even in cities, those who can fully utilize capital are not often seen. For the present plan, we should shift their capital to the path of promoting real industries. This is one point. Currently, our country still lacks capital, so we must establish various institutions to accumulate it. The women's community should establish women's banks to increase the country's capital. This is the second point. Today's economic trends are changing rapidly, and in this world of fierce commercial warfare, women in our country should cultivate basic commercial knowledge as early as possible to prepare for serving society. If this is done, there will be many leading talents in the future, and the current difficulty of lacking commercial talents in our country can also be solved easily. This is the third point. Furthermore, the so-called producers have narrow and broad definitions. According to the narrow definition, it belongs to the creation of wealth. According to the broad definition, all services to the community belong to it. If women can devote themselves to society and seek welfare for the people, they are useful talents, not just those in the agricultural and industrial classes who can be called producers. This is the fourth point.

(3) Regarding Distributors

Although distribution is not the most serious economic problem in our country today, it is still worth discussing and is closely related to the women's community. It is difficult to determine by what standards the distribution of social wealth should be based. Generally speaking, one is the aristocratic theory, which advocates that social wealth should be owned by a specific class. The inheritance system is supported by those who advocate this theory. The impropriety of this theory is obvious and does not need to be discussed in detail. The second is the socialist theory, which advocates that the distribution of social wealth should be measured according to individual needs. This theory is very reasonable, but individual needs are not easy to measure, so this theory also has aspects that are not satisfactory. The third is the liberal theory, which advocates that wealth should be distributed according to individual production capacity (contribution). Compensation is directly proportional to the size of individual contributions. This theory is based on the principle of [survival of the fittest]. It is the fairest. Although the ideal state is still far from the actual situation of our country's society, there will be a day when we enter this path in the future. If women in our country want to enjoy equality in distribution with men, they must work hard for this. There is no other way to increase one's income except through hard work. Nowadays, people in our country are accustomed to taking pride in gaining without labor, resulting in fewer and fewer producers. In the future, this bad mentality must be eradicated.

(4) Regarding Finance

At present, our country's finances are extremely corrupt. Those in power are reluctant to disclose information, and the common people ignore it. In the future, if we want to put our country's finances on the right track, the people must rise up and take on the responsibility of supervision. Women in our country must first obtain the right to participate in politics, otherwise, they will inevitably have few rights and many obligations, and they will have no way to start even if they want to supervise finances. However, how easy is it to discuss politics? It will definitely take a long period of struggle before it can become widespread. For example, the women's suffrage movement in the United States began in 1870 and did not achieve results until 1850, showing that things are not easy. To supervise finances, in our country at present, we should seek appropriate restrictions on expenditures, and also study whether the source of income is legitimate. Urge the government to implement a strict budget system, and the amount of public debt issuance should also be limited. Although women in our country are not yet able to gain any power in politics, these types of issues must be studied in advance to prepare for supervising finances in the future.

(3) Points That the Women's Community Should Pay Attention to in the Future

The responsibilities borne by women in the economy are so significant that they must fully develop their abilities and utilize their own strengths. At the same time, they must correct all weaknesses so that they can have the best of both worlds. Women in our country have many special strengths that men cannot match. To name a few major ones: (1) Precision. Women are always more precise in handling things than men. Unlike men, they are prone to making careless and impetuous mistakes. This characteristic is very suitable for modern complex economic organizations. As the world's trend dictates, the economic organizations of various countries are becoming increasingly complex. Although our country is currently based on an agricultural economy and has not fully entered the industrial age, the chaotic situation of the transitional period is not easy to handle, and commercial sentiment prediction is especially difficult. Without a calm mind and keen insight, it is not enough to talk about this. The most suitable work for women in our country, such as accounting and statistics, will definitely develop in the country in the future. (2) Morality. Women pay great attention to morality, and obeying the law is also an advantage. This is certainly due to the strict restrictions imposed by society on women's actions, but it may also be due to the self-love of the women's community itself. In our country's customs, disdain for merchants has become a habit. The main reason is that in the past, some merchants monopolized and engaged in fraudulent practices, and their morality was criticized. Therefore, society had a very bad impression of merchants, and their status in society could not be improved. (In the past, foreign scholars, such as Montesquieu of France, also rejected Chinese merchants in his writings.) In the future, when women in our country participate in various economic activities in the country, they will be able to sweep away these bad habits and correct this misconception of foreigners through factual performance. (3) Frugality. This is also a virtue of women in our country that must be maintained. Under the current circumstances in our country, it is certainly not necessary to advocate asceticism in a one-sided way to hinder the source of economic progress, but it is also necessary to recognize that all non-productive expenditures must be strictly limited, otherwise, the national livelihood will inevitably go bankrupt. Production may be new, but consumption must still conform to the principles of production. If women in our country develop the habit of frugality, it will be enough to save the country's fortunes. Moreover, women account for more than half of the country's population. If they can do their best to promote it, the results will be significant, and the national economy will definitely benefit significantly.

In addition to the above-mentioned strengths, the women's community today should also correct its own shortcomings. Today's economic competition is becoming increasingly fierce. If you want to put yourself in an invincible position, you must have a strong and persevering heart, so that you can hope to succeed in doing things. Women seem to be somewhat lacking in this regard. Furthermore, the common problem of the women's community in our country is that their vision is short-sighted. They are only limited to the present and cannot reach the future. They only care about their own interests and cannot calculate for society. This shortcoming is a major obstacle to the development of China's economy. The failure of individual careers is a minor matter. Furthermore, modern economic trends place the greatest emphasis on organization. Therefore, modern economists often add the item of organization in addition to labor, land, and capital to form the four major factors of production. Its importance can be seen. If the women's community in our country sincerely wants to occupy a superior position in China's economic society, they must find ways to enhance their organizational abilities.

Securities: Bond Market Initially Fell and Then Rose Last Week 156

From February 20th to 25th last week, the public bond market of the Huashang Securities Exchange initially saw a sharp drop in opening prices due to the apprehensive sentiment that the Rehe War would still be unavoidable. Subsequently, as the war broke out, bullish investors panicked and sold off, causing the market price to fall even more drastically. Finally, due to the impending maturity of the February futures, short positions were squeezed and prices rose. However, the intense fighting in Nanling and Beipiao and the war situation will inevitably affect the prospects of the bond market to some extent. Nevertheless, the US silver loan to China, which has been brewing for a long time, suddenly had rumors of its imminent establishment, and there were also rumors of other countries mediating a reconciliation. The financial community slightly bought in, and various groups covered their short positions, with the northern group buying particularly aggressively. Therefore, after a period of weakness, the market price showed signs of gradual recovery. Therefore, the apparent rise in market price seems to run counter to the environment, but it is actually not accidental. Monday and Tuesday happened to be the beginning of the outbreak of the Rehe War. The northern group had frantically sold off beforehand, and bullish investors panicked and sold off. The market price fell sharply for two days, with the largest drops approaching 5 yuan and the smallest drops exceeding 1 or 2 yuan. The trend was extremely unfavorable to bullish investors. As a result, short positions in the market suddenly became crowded. However, with only Wednesday and Thursday remaining for the delivery of February futures, and large bullish investors holding firm and preparing to take delivery, the news that the silver loan was expected to be established suddenly came at this time. The financial community gradually absorbed, and the short position fortifications began to shake. In addition, the rumors of reconciliation were revived, Japanese diplomacy was outwardly stern but inwardly weak, the northern group covered its shorts, and retail investors were particularly panicked, which seemed to be completely opposite to the normal track. Therefore, from Wednesday to Saturday, the trend gradually rose. The total turnover was 47,615,000 yuan. The comparison is briefly listed below to illustrate the trend. Today is a holiday for delivery and the market is closed for one day (unit: 100 yuan).

Silk and Tea Exports Face Daily Declines and Dumping of Japanese Silk 159

Last Week's Silk Market Lacked Vitality

Silk Prices Fell to Minimum Levels, European Firms Still Considered Withholding Stock to Manipulate Prices

Chinese Silk Merchants Suffered Heavy Losses; Factories Maintained Production, Awaiting Opportunities

Last week, the local Shanghai and foreign firms' silk market was completely lifeless. The Japanese exchange rate continued to decline, and Japanese silk was aggressively dumped in European and American markets at rock-bottom prices, causing the market price of Chinese silk to plummet as well. New York's B-grade white filature was quoted at only 480 taels by the China Bank's telegraphic transfer rate, while the 13/15 denier type in Lyon was only 520-530 taels. During the European war, the minimum price for white filature could still reach 630-640 taels. Prices have now fallen to the lowest level. However, European and American stockpilers still considered suppressing prices to hoard stock. Chinese silk merchants believed that silk prices could not fall any further. Moreover, they knew that the United States, angered by Japan's militaristic aggression in the Northeast, was increasingly refusing to use Japanese goods. Should the American silk weaving industry stop using Japanese silk, the sales of Chinese silk in the American market would likely increase. Therefore, they all withheld their stock and waited for an opportunity. As a result, the sales of Chinese silk last week were almost stagnant. At present, only mainland silk factories took the opportunity to purchase stock, and Indian firms replenished their stocks of yellow and rough Japanese silk, totaling 80 bales. Over 500 bales were shipped out.

New York's Raw Silk Consumption Greatly Reduced

New York has always been the center of American silk fabric production. Every time the spring silk fabric sales season starts, raw silk consumption by various silk factories inevitably increases. In recent years, the proliferation of artificial silk and the brisk sales of synthetic silk fabrics have made it difficult to expect an increase in natural silk consumption. According to news from local American silk trading firms yesterday, the total amount of raw silk consumed by silk factories throughout New York City this month (i.e., February) will not exceed 42,000-43,000 bales. Last year's February raw silk consumption totaled 45,900 bales, a decrease of 3,000-4,000 bales. It is estimated that the quantity of raw silk in stock at the end of this month will be around 67,000-68,000 bales.

Prices for Thick and Thin Raincoat Fabric are Weak 160

Raincoat fabric is currently in season for spring, and sales are brisk. Both thick and thin goods have seen considerable transactions. New varieties continue to be introduced by the trade association, with single-sided waterproof American cloth being the most active. Napped, gray elephant skin-like thin cotton cloth also enjoys wide sales. Rubberized raincoat fabric also shows a strong trend. However, their prices have been weakening due to an oversupply of goods. Yesterday, the industry was quoting 1 tael and 6 mace for the 4026 old brand single-sided waterproof American raincoat fabric. Top-grade goods of ordinary brands were quoted at 3 taels and 5 mace and a half, and second-grade goods at 3 taels and 3-4 mace.

Free Talk

An Ode to Health, A Supplement 161

— Cao Juren

Mr. Shicheng sighed at the crippled minds of people in an abnormal society and expressed boundless admiration for the health of Soviet Russia. I feel the same way. However, China cannot be compared to Europe and America. They are standing on the line of death, while we have already died. What appears is wandering souls and ghosts. Fundamentally speaking, there is no health to speak of!

"How can one avoid the sorrows and resentments of life?" I agree with this statement. How can we answer the "sorrows and resentments of life?" For thousands of years, sages, heroes, literati, and scholars have only had the following three ways: "My heart is sorrowful, anxiously like pounding: I feign sleep with perpetual worry, worrying makes me old; my heart is full of melancholy, and sickness is like a headache." (Poetry, Xiaobian) This is the first way: sorrowing until old age, without any hope. "Have you not seen the bright mirror in the high hall grieving over white hair, in the morning like black silk, in the evening becoming snow?" "In life, one should enjoy every pleasure, do not let the golden goblet face the moon in vain!" This is the second way: dancing, drinking, and letting the years pass by. "Hoo-hoo, you finish singing, I take the stage, mistaking another place for my hometown. How absurd!" In the end, it is all making wedding clothes for others! This is the third way: it is destined to be so, and everything is in vain. When we look at literary works, no matter what form they take, their fundamental concepts, apart from this individualism of "sorrow," "decadent enjoyment," and "predestination," is there any other healthy consciousness? Apart from numbing the youth to make them complacent with the status quo, is there any other effect? Flying to and fro, gray owls hoot the death knell of the Chinese nation! Have the new literary writers since the May Fourth Movement jumped out of this circle?

"No Struggle, No Drama." I am deeply moved by the words of this great critic. If we cannot answer life with a positive attitude, if we cannot experience the "joy of life," and if we cannot understand a nation with the power of a collective, I am afraid that we will never have life and will forever be reduced to wandering souls and ghosts!

Liwa Lida Village 162

— Mu Shiying

That day was the Dragon Boat Festival! Such great weather! But in the city, the sky is not blue enough, and the sun is not bright enough. Pei Pei and I went to Liwa Lida to find a wider field, a taller sky, and the youngest moment of one o'clock. Leaving the city in the city, we arrived in the suburbs in the early summer breeze. After crossing the Suzhou River, there was a very long path with willows on both sides, their branches dragging straight to the ground. After walking the path, we saw a field of grass, a river, a red house, a bandstand, and white tablecloths, black coffee, a row of old trees swaying in the breeze, and some dreams.

Over there, the wheat fields stretched straight from the edge of the village to the horizon. On the horizon, there was a tree with a crow's nest, next to a pile of fences, a black tiled house, and from there, the Liwa Lida River gently rolled to the edge of the village.

We rowed a narrow, double-oared boat into the middle of the water, letting it drift with the current. It was a flowing sky, without clouds. A warm breeze brought the double song of the cuckoo from the horizon, blowing, blowing, from horizon to horizon, from wheat field to wheat field. The wind, the song, floated to the wheat ears, floated to the surface of the water, and then dissipated like smoke in Pei Pei's hair.

She sighed softly. I smiled.

Next to the boat, a hundred geese slept on the ripples, their heads tucked under their wings. In front, a Russian man was also rowing a boat. Quiet water, quiet sky, quiet fields, quiet boat, even the back in the white shirt exposed on the edge of the boat was quiet. Only the two oars rose and fell together. Pei Pei's face had sunlight, a dark and delicate red face, a healthy face. My nose also had sunlight, and I took a deep breath, wanting to absorb it. I smiled. She sighed again.

It was not easy to see her sitting so quietly. Her brown eyes were transparent, with an intense fragrance, intense light and shadow. But today, her eyes were a pair of dreams, darker and deeper than usual. She also did not laugh as loudly or speak as loudly as usual.

A sound of a guitar drifted from the shore, quietly. I lit a cigarette. The smoke slowly drifted into the willow branches. It was dusk. In the twilight, I saw her pupils turn black, staring at me. I thought, thinking of when I first met her.

We will only return when we are sitting on the moon! The moon topped the head of the Russian man rowing in front, he had bald hair, rowing two silver oars.

Poor Child 163

— Ms. Peng Xuezhen

"Poor child! You don't want people to call you that," but don't pout your little mouth, you should learn to be more patient!

Yesterday, I received a letter from your sister from Nanning, and I was really surprised that she ran so far. She told me that she had no choice but to leave you, Minmin, at home, which made her very sad. I also sighed for you when I heard that!

You probably don't remember: one summer two years ago, I came to your house for the first time, and also only this once, to see Minmin, whom I had wanted to see for a long time. At that time, you were barefoot, being punished by them, sitting on a mat. It was terribly hot, and you were only wearing a sweaty undershirt, exposing your small, flabby arms. You were clamoring to get off the ground, but they wouldn't let you wear shoes. You were really stubborn, you refused to call me. I still can't forget your lively little eyes, the little eyes that turned into a line when you smiled. Your sister took me around Nanhu. You wanted to come along, but she stubbornly refused. After we walked out the door, you were carried in by the old nanny. I could still hear your loud cries from afar. You must have been thinking: my sister only cares about her friends and not Minmin, right?

At Yanyu Tower, I said, "Minmin is too pitiful!" Your sister didn't say anything, just sighed softly. Minmin, from her deeply furrowed brow, I could see how much she loved you!

The year before last, your sister came, taking a stroll around Canglang Pavilion, looking at the distant fields and the blue sky. She was thinking about you again. The aunt didn't like Minmin's bad temper, told you to be a good boy. But Minmin raised her small face and said seriously, "Minmin has no mom!" You said it so well! You really have it in you, Minmin. A six- or seven-year-old child can say such words. You understand the loneliness of a child without a mother's love. Do you remember your mother who died two years ago? Good, you should always remember her. That is what you should do!

You are a clever child, often uttering words from your little mouth that are more innocent and profound than adults. So your sister often said, "This child needs someone to carefully take care of, too clever."

Isn't that so? Your father also died the year before last, and your older siblings all work, so you follow them everywhere. A six-year-old child lives in kindergarten. It is said that you are very good there, but too restrained, not so lively. Are you too sensible, or are the other children bullying you? Minmin, tell me!

Your sister has now gone far away, and there are fewer relatives around you. You can't help looking for your sister everywhere when you come back from school, right? She has gone to that southern country full of bananas and palm trees. Have you cried about this?

Do you admit that you are a poor child? You should firmly shake your little head: Minmin is not poor! Minmin has older brothers who care for her, older sisters who love her, and aunts who like her! You are smart, yes, so you have to understand more things: there are many poor children in this world. Have you seen the children in the neighborhood who don't have enough to eat or wear? You should study hard, play hard, and the days without hardship are in the future! Show some courage, look at this world that is more ferocious than the tiger mask your sister bought you, then you will know if you are a poor child!

Smile! Have the small trees in the yard sprouted? Children are as hopeful as those green sprouts, especially our poor children!

A Black Woman's Quest for God (12) 164

— by Xiao Boner, translated by Yi Xian

The sorcerer was stunned, but he immediately smiled at Ge Di. He replied, "Let's not make this a personal matter, shall we?"

"However, if it's not a personal matter, it's meaningless," the black girl said. "If I were to do as you tell me,"

"What should I do! I tell you that I love you! Don't you feel that I am being impudent?"

"Of course not," the sorcerer said. "You mustn't think like that. Although you are black and I am white, we are equal before the God who created us like this."

"I didn't think like that," the black girl said. "When I spoke, I didn't say that I am a black person and you are just a pitiful white person. Please treat me as a white queen and yourself as a white king. What does it matter? Why are you staring blankly?"

"There, there," the sorcerer said. "Oh, I am the most pitiful of all pitiful white people; but I also regard myself" as a king. This is when people's evil forces me to go mad."

"I've seen even worse kings," the black girl said; "You don't need to be ashamed. Oh, oh, like in the Bible, you" be King Solomon, and I'll be the Queen of Sheba. I came to you to say that I love you. That means coming to possess you. I embrace the lioness's to eat you, to make you a part of myself. From now on, you can only think of things that make me happy, and not of things that make you happy. I will stand between you and yourself, between you and God. Isn't this terrible tyranny? Love is something that devours people. Can you imagine a heaven within which there is love?"

"There is nothing else in my heaven. What else is heaven besides love?" the sorcerer said boldly, but also uncomfortably.

"There is also glory. That is the image of God, the home of God's thoughts: there is no flirtatious style, no lingering like lice clinging to the body of a sheep. I The pastor is talking about love; but she avoids all her lovers, and works for God. Those white people turn their eyes away when they see me, fearing that they will fall in love with me. There are groups of men and women who are devoted to God's work, calling themselves brothers and sisters, but they don't even speak to each other."

"They see through," the sorcerer said.

"Of course, this is stupid," the black girl said. "We have to live with people, we have to be satisfied with"

"That's it. However, our souls need solitude, just as our bodies need love, isn't that obvious? We need each other's physical help and each other's spiritual help: but our souls have to be alone with God; whenever people come to love you, to want your soul, your spirit, and your body, you say like this, 'Don't come close: I belong to myself, not to you.' That kind of 'love argument, for me who is seeking God, is more insulting'" than for a warrior who must fight against slavery and murder, or for a hunter who must kill or see his children starve."

"Then, can I say 'You must kill each other; this is the commandment given to you'?" the sorcerer said.

"That's just turning the previous statement around, [the black girl said. [It is not a law of life. To be honest with you, this kind of cure-all commandment of yours is like the pills sold to us by quacks: it's useful one out of twenty times, and it's useless nineteen times. Moreover, I am not seeking commandments. I am seeking God."

"Continue seeking, may God be with you," the sorcerer said. "You must pass through me to find such a God, go" searching," he said, and then he disappeared.

"This is probably your specialty," the black girl said; "But I'm a little sad that I lost you; because I feel in my heart" that you are a lovely man, and you have a good heart."

She went another mile and met an old fisherman carrying a huge church on his shoulders.

"Panning for Gold in the Sea" 165

— Zhuang Zhen

Green sea, blue sea, stormy sea, shining with the golden sun, the silver moon… From ancient times to the present, how many poets and writers have praised this, giving them how much comfort, how much encouragement, and how many feelings! However, what scientists see in the sea seems to be completely different from what poets see!

According to many scientists, the sea, which has become the source of "poetic emotions" for poets and writers, is the world's largest treasure trove, and we can pan out brilliant gold and silver from the sea. Their research shows that every ton of seawater contains ten milligrams of silver, so if we calculate the total amount of seawater in the world at 127 million cubic . And the total population of the world is 1.5 billion, each person can get a silver block worth 9 million yuan to distribute. As for the gold content, it is even more than silver, and it is said that every ton of seawater contains an average of 50 milligrams of gold, so if it is distributed according to the total population of the world mentioned above, each person can get a gold block of 48,000 grams!

Friends, do you say you are poor? However, the property that you should be allocated is so much, but it is scattered in the sea!

"Panning for gold in the sea", who can still laugh at this! Some chemists who dream of gold have been engaged in the research of "recovering gold from seawater" and "recovering silver from seawater" for several years, and are still constantly doing experiments!

Vow to Save the Nation and Fight the Enemy to the Death 172

Ju Zheng's Report at the National Government Memorial Week

Chairman Lin led the proceedings, and Ju Zheng delivered a report entitled "Vow to Save the Nation and Fight the Enemy to the Death," stating that in recent days, the anti-Japanese soldiers in Rehe have been fighting the enemy to the death. All Chinese people are eager to take action because the evil demons of East Asia have betrayed their race and the ancestors of their culture and harmed their fellow countrymen. If the people of the nation all vow together, those with wealth will contribute wealth, and those with ability will contribute ability, to achieve the goal of saving the world and the nation. The key to fighting to the death lies in being able to act, being strong and persistent, and being calm. All countries in the world are paying close attention to our engagement with the enemy. The government and the actions of the people should be very cautious. From the beginning of the attack on Rehe, Japan has been promoting the blockade of our ports, even disturbing North China with threats. We will not panic because of this, nor will we be negligent in our determination to fight to the death, to engage in a protracted war. After three to five months, when the cunning plans of the violent Japanese are frustrated, and other countries take advantage of their weaknesses and impose sanctions, Japan will inevitably submit, and the East Asian incident will come to a small conclusion. Otherwise, it will inevitably trigger a world war, and the result will be that the violent Japanese will be the first to fall. We must not harbor any thoughts of侥幸, persevere, and the deeper the pain, the more steadfast our struggle. When all the people are united, this is the true meaning of fighting to the death. Comrades, let us vow to save the nation and fight Japan to the death, and next year today, we will have a commemorative celebration of our success in resisting Japan. (London) It has been rumored from the Far East by the Japanese that British Foreign Secretary Simon allegedly stated to Japan that if Japanese actions were limited to Rehe, the British government would not oppose Japanese actions in Rehe. It is verified that this news was transmitted by the Japanese United Press, which stated that before starting the attack on Rehe, the Japanese Foreign Minister inquired about the attitudes of the British, American, French, Italian, and German ambassadors stationed in Tokyo. Of these five countries, only Britain replied that if the Japanese-Manchurian army's operations did not go beyond the scope of Rehe Province, the British government had no objections to this action.

In addition to the British Foreign Office formally denying this news, I (the reporter claims himself) also learned that the British government unequivocally supports the League of Nations' resolution that Japanese troops should withdraw from Manchuria, and also learned that the American government has agreed with Britain's position on this matter.

Regarding the proposal to ban the shipment of arms to China and Japan, news has been received from official circles that the British government has refused to allow a ban specifically against Japan, because any arms shipped to China are likely to be seized by the Japanese fleet, so this plan is very difficult to implement.

US Congress Passes Emergency Banking Act 178

Restrictions on Withdrawals

Averts Financial Crisis

Reuters, New York, 26th: The case to authorize the Currency Administrator to restrict withdrawals from all $17,000,000,000 of deposits in over six thousand banks in the United States was passed in both the Senate and the House of Representatives yesterday and was signed and approved today by President Hoover, thus becoming law. The banking crisis in Maryland and Michigan is also being followed by President-elect Roosevelt and future Secretary of State Hull. The Washington Financial Good Samaritans are considering lending to banks in Baltimore and Detroit. According to a report from Lima, Ohio, the First American Trust Company decided to allow withdrawals of two percent of deposits. Yesterday, the Governor of Maryland announced a three-day holiday for all banks and financial institutions in the state to facilitate the resolution of measures to curb the large number of withdrawals. The eight-day period of bank holidays in Michigan has now been extended.

Reuters, New York, 26th: Following the banking crises in Michigan and Maryland, discussions are now taking place throughout the United States on authorizing governors to declare suspensions of payments to protect banks and depositors. Today, legislative assemblies in twenty states are meeting to discuss ways to deal with this trend. The governors of Indiana, Arkansas, and Wisconsin have now signed bills authorizing the declaration of suspensions of payments if necessary. At the same time, New York and New Jersey, among five other states, have passed new laws increasing the power of officials to assist banks in maintaining operations and facilitating reorganization. Four banks in Arkansas, with a total of $5 million in deposits, have now been merged into the National Commercial Bank and Trust Company. Five clearing houses in Ohio, with a total of $55 million in deposits, are now restricting the withdrawal of savings deposits to no more than one percent per month. As for commercial current accounts, the amount of withdrawals is limited to the average amount withdrawn in recent months.

Japan's National Debt 184

Reaches Over Eight Billion

(Beiping) A person from Tokyo said that according to the latest statistics from the Japanese Ministry of Finance, the country's national debt has reached over eight billion. Now, it is further invading Rehe, and the financial situation is becoming increasingly unsustainable. The Japanese zaibatsu have occupied the Northeast, and the annual maintenance cost is about 40 to 50 million, which is extremely difficult. As a result of the Japanese zaibatsu's militarism, Japan's rural areas are increasingly collapsing. The total amount of debt owed by farmers has exceeded 1.2 billion yuan. There are approximately 5.57 million farming households nationwide, with an average debt of 1,200 to 1,300 yuan per household. The annual interest on the debt is about 110 yuan. The income from agricultural products is not enough to pay off the debt. The price of agricultural products is falling daily. Before the European War, the highest price of Japanese silk was about 4,000 yuan per province, but now it has fallen to 400 yuan. The price of rice was at its highest 50 yuan, but now it has fallen to 20 yuan. The cost of rice per stone and taxes combined is about 21 yuan. Farm children account for 83% of the total number of soldiers in the country, so it affects the instability of the military's morale. The Tokyo Stock Exchange has even had five days of closure. The gold standard has now fallen from more than three yuan to nine jiao. Amid the rural bankruptcy and economic panic, the Japanese zaibatsu are still actively conscripting soldiers. Those who are conscripted are mostly pampered and afraid of death. The Japanese government is also concerned about the high number of Japanese soldiers dying, because it feels unable to raise funds for the compensation of the dead. Yonghe Industrial Company's Boiler Explodes 194

Many Male and Female Workers Injured

A Loud Explosion Shakes the Vicinity

Seventeen Injured and One Dead Already Known

The Exact Number of Dead and Injured Still Awaits Further Investigation

At 11:30 AM this morning, at the Yonghe Industrial Company in West Baoxing Road, Zhabei, the rubber factory's boiler exploded due to electrical leakage and carelessness. The loud explosion shook the vicinity. At the time, hundreds of male and female workers were working and fled in panic upon hearing the news. The Zhabei Fourth Fire Brigade rushed to the rescue and successively rescued seventeen injured male and female workers and pulled out the body of a female worker. As of the time this newspaper went to press, rescue efforts were still underway, and the exact number of dead and injured is still under investigation. The details of the accident are recorded below:

Rubber Factory's Carelessness 195

The Yonghe Industrial Company on West Baoxing Road, Zhabei, was founded in 1918 and was originally a cosmetics manufacturing company. It began to operate a rubber factory in 1930, manufacturing rubber shoes, rubber balls, and other products. During the January 28th Incident last year, many of the factory's buildings were destroyed by bombing, and the inventory was also burned to the ground, resulting in a loss of 800,000 to 900,000 yuan. After the Japanese troops withdrew, the factory worked to restore the factory site on West Baoxing Road in Zhabei, which was entirely used as a rubber factory, while the cosmetics factory was moved to Kang Nao Te Road. The entire rubber factory has approximately 300 female workers and 200 male workers. The business is considered quite good. At around 11:30 AM this morning, some of the workers had already left work, while others were still working.

Four Loud Explosions 196

Suddenly, the boiler exploded due to electrical leakage. The loud explosion sounded like artillery fire, followed by flames. All four of the factory's boilers were affected one after another, and the sound shook the vicinity. Nearby residents thought that another major incident had occurred and came out to investigate. At the time, the factory was engulfed in flames, and the Zhabei Fourth Fire Brigade rushed to the rescue, making efforts to rescue male and female workers from danger. By this time, most of the workers had escaped to safety, with only a few trapped in the flames, crying for help. The firefighters then successively rescued seventeen injured male and female workers. This reporter rushed to investigate at around 1:00 PM this afternoon. The factory's thick smoke had not yet dissipated, and the firefighters were still continuing their rescue efforts and pulling out the body of a female worker. Her face was blurred, making it difficult to identify her. It is expected that more will be found, so the exact number of dead and injured still awaits the factory's final investigation.

Losses of Tens of Thousands of Yuan 197

This reporter visited the factory authorities and was told that all four boilers had been completely destroyed, but the inventory had not yet been affected, with losses of around 30,000 to 40,000 yuan. The factory has been working to recover since the war, and it is unfortunate that it has suffered another disaster. The dead and injured male and female workers will be given generous compensation for medical treatment and care. An active investigation is currently underway. The number of dead and injured can only be known accurately after the flames are completely extinguished.

Injured Persons' Names 198

Wang Gengquan, age 42, from Wuxi (resident of No. 5, Chunyang Lane, Baoxing Road), suffered burns all over his body, his condition quite serious. His wife, Ms. Shen, injured her hand. Gao Quangui, age 39, from Wuxi, injured his head, body, hands, and feet. Shi Agui, age 38, from Jiangyin, injured his head. Liu Zhaodi (female worker), age 27, from Jiangyin, injured her head, hands, and body. The above five persons were all sent to Baolong Hospital for treatment. Hua Li Shi, age 31, from Jiangsu, suffered injuries all over her body, her condition critical. Gu Amei, age 19, injured her head. Li Caifeng, age 20, injured her head. Zhu Zhao Shi, age 50, injured her head. Hu Jinmei, age 21, injured her hands and feet. Pan Pu Shi, age 40, suffered scalding all over her body. Chen Xu Shi, age 40, suffered gradual injuries all over her body. The above two persons were hospitalized. Guo Sumei, age 20, Wang Amei, age 28, Xu Sanmei, age 19, Wang Linbao, age 24, Shen Rendi, age 22, and Zhu Amei, age 23, all injured their heads and were soon able to be discharged from the hospital. Male worker Zhu Jinshui, age 40, injured his head. Jin Bentou, age 20, injured his head and hands. Hu Shaoquan, age 26, injured his head and hands. Nie Shengkai, age 15, injured his hands and head. Zhu Jiangping, age 16, injured his hands and head. Yang Faxin, age 22, Qiu Zhengyou, age 34, injured his head. Wu Yuanzhang, age 36, injured his head. Chen Yigen, age 37, injured his head, hands, and feet, his condition quite critical. Liu Jiangyou, age 25, injured his entire body. The above male and female injured persons were all transported by vehicle to Renji Hospital for medical treatment.

Japanese Set Up Armory in Shanghai 208

Naval Ministry Has Dispatched a Large Number of Craftsmen to Shanghai

Dalian Company Cancels Shanghai Route

Military Industry Comes to Shanghai: After the construction of the new barracks for the Japanese Naval Landing Forces in Shanghai, Chief Commander Sugisaka telegraphed the Naval Ministry, requesting the addition of an armory in Shanghai dedicated to manufacturing and repair. The Naval Ministry has approved it and immediately transferred a large number of technicians from the Sasebo Naval Arsenal, including Yoshida, Iwanaga Katsushi, Sasaki, Sakamoto, Hirata Tsuyoshi, Kajiki Kiyofumi, Ide, Gota, Ono, Hayashida, Kitajima, Matsumoto, and more than 30 others. Carrying machinery parts for manufacturing weapons, they arrived in Shanghai by Japanese ship today. Major General Sugisaka has dispatched them to the new barracks in Hongkou to install the machinery, which will be dedicated to repairing and manufacturing military supplies for the Japanese Navy in Shanghai and the Yangtze River.

Japanese Ships Transport: Since the outbreak of the hot war, Japanese ships from Dalian Kisen and Tianjin will, from this day forward, change to the Dalian-Tianjin route, canceling the Shanghai route and being assigned for transportation during the military period. They will also be prepared to provide transportation to Dalian for Japanese residents in Peiping and Tianjin when they evacuate if necessary. Therefore, from today, the company has stopped selling passenger tickets to Tianjin and stopped loading goods to Tianjin.

Negotiations on Inspecting Concession Factories 209

The Municipal Council Expresses Approval in Principle

Other Opinions Will Be Responded to in Writing

Regarding the municipal government's inspection of factories in the concessions, this morning, according to Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, in order to implement the factory inspection of the Factory Law promulgated by the central government, the concession side has not yet implemented it due to unresolved negotiations. Recently, I again met with Mr. Fessenden, Director-General of the Municipal Council, and stated that the municipal government urgently needs to start inspecting the factories in the concessions. Mr. Fessenden expressed support for the principle of inspecting factories, but the Municipal Council also had opinions to express and promised to respond in writing in the shortest possible time. No response has been received yet. The content will be studied after the response is received, and a decision will be made on future procedures. As for the tragic case of the Zhengtai Rubber Factory, it is said that the factory has offered compensation of 300 yuan per victimized worker. The resolution of this matter may not be so simple. The cause of the disaster should be investigated first, and then the issue of compensation should be considered. As for the issues of building roads beyond the boundary and promoting the new system of weights and measures in the concessions, they are all in active progress.

Postal Parcels Sold Must Be Declared 210

The Jianghai Customs announced today that, starting from March 1st, all imported postal parcels and other items shipped in postal items, if for sale, must be provided with a formal import list and submitted to the parcel staff stationed at the customs office for verification. Items loaded in postal parcels, if for personal use and not for sale, do not need to be declared.

National Arts Performance Filmed for Chicago Expo 211

The Central Guoshu Institute Is Under Preparation

The Central Guoshu Institute was established in 1928 and has been in operation for five years. The museum is currently preparing to hold a five-year anniversary celebration and plans to film the national arts performance and send it to the Chicago Exposition for screening. According to Ong Guoxun, Advisor of the Central Guoshu Institute, speaking to the Central News Agency reporter, at this time of national crisis, the Central Guoshu Institute, in order to awaken the people of the country to exercise their bodies and strive for the country, plans to hold a five-year anniversary celebration to expand publicity and arouse the attention of the people of the country to national arts. It is now actively preparing to be held in Beijing in late March. As for the upcoming Chicago Exposition in the United States, the Central Guoshu Institute originally planned to send personnel to participate, but because the round-trip travel expenses are very high, it has now been decided to film the national arts performance and send it to the conference for screening.

Jiangsu Rice Association Asks to Stop the Rice Transport Strike 212

The Jiangsu Ninghu Municipal and County Rice Industry Association held its 16th standing meeting of the second session at Zuo Xiutang yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. Because not enough members from various counties attended, the quorum was not met, and it was changed to a discussion meeting. Chairman Zhao Zixin reported that the strike in Shanghai had not been resolved, which was very unfortunate. At present, it is heard that there are more than 100 rice boats carrying rice from the interior to Shanghai that have been blocked on the way. Over time, it is feared that the rice will overheat. Moreover, Shanghai's rice supply depends on the interior. If this continues, it is feared that there will be a panic in the people's food supply, which will have a significant impact on social safety and stability. It is appropriate to request the authorities not to condone it any further and to strictly stop it to prevent the matter from expanding and hindering the people's food supply. It was publicly decided to request the Social Bureau to stop it immediately. In addition, the Changshu County Chamber of Commerce sent a letter requesting that the dispute over the price of rice be banned. It has been forwarded to the Bean and Rice Industry Association for reply and will be replied to by the association later.

Brazilian National Sells Handguns at Dadong Hotel 214

Secret Hand-Off in the Urinal

Customer Turns Out to Be Detective

Detective Hua Men of the Huishi Patrol Room received a report from an informant a few days ago stating that a Westerner was secretly selling handguns in the Dadong Hotel on Yinghua Street. He sent Detective Deng Shu to pretend to be a customer and secretly contacted the Westerner once. He stated that each handgun and 100 bullets would cost 220 yuan and agreed to exchange the money on the 25th of this month. On the due date, Chinese and Western detectives waited in the billiard room upstairs in the Dadong Hotel. As expected, the Westerner was already there. Detective Deng immediately went up to greet him and then went to the urinal together. The Westerner immediately took out an [A. C. Tirera] brand handgun, one hundred bullets, and a bullet case from his side and handed them to the Chinese detective. The Western detective Hua Men immediately arrested him and took him to the patrol room. After questioning, his name was [Isique Gestin], age 30, a Brazilian. He was ordered to be detained. This morning, he was escorted to the 8th Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. Patrol Room lawyer Wang Yaotang stated that he was currently prosecuting the defendant under Article 201, Section 1 of the Criminal Law, but all the guns and bullets had not yet been sent to the Council for verification, so he requested a postponement. According to the Chinese and Western detectives' complaint, the defendant confessed that the matter was done by another Westerner, Si Huituo. After Judge Qian Wenqi verified the confession, he instructed that the defendant Isique Gestin be detained pending rescheduling of the trial next Friday.

Both Sentenced to Remand Pending Investigation and Retrial

Hongkou Patrol Room Detective Chief Wei Jinfu, Detectives Yang Zhaoqing, Liu Zhaonian, Wang Runhe, and Detective Zhang Faxiang learned that robbers were hiding in a house at No. 25 Ximen Road, French Concession. They confessed that there were still robbers at No. 276 Hede Road. They also arrested Shao Xing native Tang Agen, Ningbo native Xu Changgen, Cai Xiangyun, and woman Li Cai Shi and seized two handguns and fifteen bullets. They were all taken back to the patrol room and detained separately. This morning, they were escorted to the 3rd Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. Patrol Room lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the previous situation and stated that the two handguns were loaded with bullets and it was not known where they were going to rob. He requested that they be detained temporarily to investigate the defendants' crimes and that the handguns be submitted for inspection. After Judge Wu Zehan briefly questioned the defendants Rong and others, he instructed that they still be remanded separately and rescheduled for investigation and trial. Also, Huishan Patrol Room Detectives Liu Baoshan and Yin Zhanqing and Western Detective Watson arrested robbers Changshu native Wei Shixiang, Wuxi native Zhang Fugeng, Danyang native Zhou Tonghai, Shanghai native Hu Shanqing, and Chongming native A Liu and five others yesterday afternoon at Shenzhou Hotel at No. 159 Zhejiang Road, China Hotel at No. 91 Jiujiang Road, and Zhongnan Hotel on Beijing Road.
