Some Overbearing Soldiers in Japan (Tokyo Correspondence) 217

The Japanese people's worship of soldiers and belief in force probably began with the Russo-Japanese War. At that time, Japan, an island country, defeated Russia, which dominated the Eurasian continent. Its heroic image can be imagined. This is the general reason why Japanese warlords were able to be overbearing and militarism was able to become the belief center of the entire nation. Therefore, Japanese soldiers became a special class among the people of the whole country. The backgrounds and deeds of army figures such as Chief of Staff Prince Kan'in, Minister of the Army Araki Sadao, Director General of Education Hayashi Senjuro, Director of Army Aviation Watanabe Jotaro, Director of Army Technology Ogata Katsuichi, and Commander of the Kwantung Army Muto Nobuyoshi are already familiar to the world, so there is no need to say more. Now we want to briefly talk about the secondary army figures in the Japanese military.

(1) Graduates of the 9th Class of the Military Academy

Graduates of the 9th class of the Japanese Army Military Academy have a special advantage in the military. For example, Lieutenant Generals Masaki, Honjo, Abe, Matsui, Araki, Hayashi, Yamamoto, and others all hold important positions and are important figures in the Japanese Army and are recognized as the dominating figures in the future army. Masaki Jinzaburo, former Commander of the Taiwan Army and currently Vice Chief of Staff, is said to be able to be promoted to general this year. In the near future, he will surely be honored as Chief of Staff. Honjo Shigeru, the notorious creator of the September 18th Incident and the incubator of [Manchukuo], formerly Commander of the Kwantung Army. Last July, he was transferred back to the country and appointed Military Councilor. He will surely be promoted to general this year and will also be a major figure in the Japanese military in the future. Abe Nobuyuki, currently Commander of the Taiwan Army, served as [Minister Without Portfolio] during the Hamaguchi Cabinet. During the illness of Army Minister Ugaki, he served as Acting Army Minister, and he can be said to be the actual Army Minister. Since the retirement of General Ugaki, Abe should be the successor of that faction. Abe is one of the most powerful candidates for Army Minister in the near future. Matsui Ishigen was the Japanese Plenipotentiary Representative sent to Geneva to participate in the Disarmament Conference and served as the Second Department Chief of the General Staff Headquarters and the Commander of the 11th Division.

(2) Future Talents of the General Staff Headquarters

Major General Umezu Yoshijiro, Chief of the General Affairs Department of the General Staff Headquarters, is a graduate of the 15th class of the Military Academy. He graduated first in his class from Kumamoto Army Elementary School when he was young. Major General Furushō Mikio, Chief of the First Department, was the first graduate of the 14th class. Major General Nagata Tetsuzan, Chief of the Second Department, served as the Chief of the Military Affairs Section of the Army Ministry and personally observed the general mobilization measures of various countries during the European War. He is now regarded by the Japanese as an expert in the Japanese national general mobilization plan. Major General Ogawa Toshishiro, Chief of the Third Department, is known as [Army Minister Araki's confidant] and is expected to be the future Chief of Staff. Major General Nishio Toshizo, Chief of the Fourth Department, is a graduate of the 14th class of the Military Academy. He served as the Chief of the First Section of the Education Directorate and has a deep understanding of military education. He is quite hopeful of becoming the next Director of Education. The above five people are important and promising talents in the General Staff Headquarters.

(3) Future Talents of the Naval General Staff

Vice Admiral Yanagawa Heisuke, Vice Chief of the Naval General Staff, is from the cavalry department of the 17th class of the Military Academy and is the most trusted figure of Army Minister Araki. Major General Yamaoka Juatsu, Chief of the Military Affairs Bureau, is, like Vice Chief Yanagawa, a person who was specially promoted and reused by Mr. Araki. Yamaoka was on the staff of Nogi's army during the Russo-Japanese War. The Japanese praised him for succeeding Tanaka Giichi, Ugaki Kazunari, Tata Hitaro, Abe Nobuyuki, and Sugiyama Gen as a [soldier with a politician's mind]. He first served as the Chief of the Second Section of the Education Directorate and then as the Brigade Commander of the First Infantry Brigade. When Army Minister Araki took office, he was awarded the important position of Chief of the Military Affairs Bureau. Colonel Yamashita Tomoyuki, Chief of the Military Affairs Section of the famous Army Ministry for a time, is a graduate of the 18th class. Finally, we must also mention the head of the press group, Colonel Honma Masaharu. Since the establishment of the press group, he has been promoted as the first head of the group, and he is likely to develop greatly in military and political aspects in the future.

(4) Future Talents of the Education Directorate

Lieutenant General Kashii Kohei, Director of the Education Directorate, is a graduate of the 12th class of the Military Academy and the former Commander of the Japanese Army in North China. He was the instigator of the Tianjin Incident. According to the usual Japanese custom, after serving as the Director of the Education Directorate, they will soon take over the great power, such as Ugaki Kazunari, Kishimoto Shikatarō, Hayashi Senjuro, and Araki Sadao, which are its precedents. Therefore, Kashii's promotion will inevitably be no exception. Lieutenant General Tada Shunroku, Chief of Artillery, graduated in the same year as Kashii. Although his current position is still low, his future is absolutely hopeful. He is the younger brother of the late Dada Hitaro. From the artillery department, he has served as the Brigade Commander of the 4th Field Heavy Artillery Brigade and the Chief of the 4th and 1st Departments of the General Staff Headquarters. He is a military strategist and one of the few famous generals in the Education Directorate. In the near future, he will also be promoted to Vice Chief of Staff.

(5) Generals in Battle

Among the division commanders of the Japanese Army, Lieutenant General Niiya Harushige, Commander of the 5th Division, is the most famous. Niiya served as Vice Chief of Staff and Chief of the General Affairs Department of the General Staff Headquarters. He is a graduate of the 12th class of the Military Academy and an outstanding talent of the General Staff Headquarters. During the transition of the Ugaki system, he was at his post in Hiroshima, and then he was transferred to work in the Ministry. Lieutenant General Sugiyama Gen, Commander of the 12th Division, graduated from the Military Academy in the same year as Niiya. He served as the Chief of the Military Affairs Bureau and the Vice Minister of the Army. When the Ugaki system was handed over, he had already taken office as the division commander, and he is quite hopeful of becoming an attendant military officer or the Director of Education. Lieutenant General Koiso Kuniaki, Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army, is a graduate of the 12th class. During the Saito Cabinet, Araki recognized him and promoted him to Chief of the Military Affairs Bureau. Later, when Muto took office as the Commander of the Kwantung Army, Koiso was promoted to Chief of Staff. Major General Okamura Yasuji, a graduate of the 16th class of the Military Academy. During the Shanghai Incident, General Shirakawa was ordered to serve as the Commander of the Shanghai Expeditionary Force, and Okamura was promoted to Deputy Chief of Staff. Colonel Saito Yūhei, currently a senior staff officer, may have great development in the Japanese Army in the future. The above five people are regarded by the Japanese military as outstanding talents in the battlefield.

In addition, there is Lieutenant General Tatekawa Yoshitsugu, who served as the Chief of the 1st Department of the General Staff Headquarters and was later sent to Geneva to attend the Disarmament Conference as a military representative. Today, all Japanese people regard him as an outstanding talent dispatched overseas.

Random Remarks

Echoes of Promoting Female Police Officers 218

— Geng

Since various newspapers published the news that "the Ministry of Interior Affairs on the 16th issued a consultation to provincial governments requesting the promotion of female police officers," a group of people who view women with a special "X-ray" perspective were even more astonished than they were a few years ago when they suddenly heard the news of women taking the county magistrate examination. Because women taking the county magistrate examination was an unprecedented innovation, let's leave that aside for now, but when they take office, according to the regulations on addressing county officials as "Your Honor," how should the common people address them? And how should they address "him"? This had already perplexed these people. Now, the issue of promoting female police officers, although it follows in the footsteps of Europe and America, ultimately feels like it has flown in from outer space in our esteemed country. How can it not cause them great alarm?

In reality, the wheel of progress, which adapts to the needs of society and conforms to the trends of the world, will not stop because of some reactionary forces. Upon hearing this news, some young people in the female community openly discussed it with excitement, reaching the conclusion: "If we're going to do it, let's join the volunteer army so that we can kill the enemy like the soldiers on the front lines!" What heroic words that liberate the female community. Hearing them, one cannot help but feel a sense of "The wind is howling, the Yi River is cold!"

China's population is said to be 470 million, but in reality, if half of the female compatriots do not unanimously arm themselves with a shared hatred for the enemy, then will the slogan of "national mobilization to jointly face national crisis" not turn into "national semi-mobilization"?

If we flip through ancient national history, for example, Mulan's twelve years of military service, the Tang Dynasty Princess Pingyang's "Women's Army" that helped Emperor Taizong secure the empire, Liang Hongyu's personal drumming to assist in battle and sharing labor with soldiers, and Qin Liangyu's courage, horsemanship, archery, and repeated suppression of rebellions, these are all brilliantly recorded female war achievements that have become beautiful tales throughout the ages. As for the news of a nameless female general riding a white horse in the Northeast Volunteer Army last year who fought bravely and died, it is also well-known in the world. That is even more proof that meritorious service is not exclusive to men, and even women can courageously kill the enemy!

"If we're going to do it, let's join the volunteer army so that we can kill the enemy like the soldiers on the front lines!" Under this slogan of sorrowful and heroic spirit, enough to shake mountains and rivers, many other ambitious young women should rise up in response, immediately go to the front lines to do practical work, or organize ambulance teams. We should prepare sacrificial lambs and fine wine to sincerely send them off on their heroic journey!

Bees and Deer Without Honey 219

— Lin

Buzz buzz buzz

A poet wrote this motto on his desk: "Woman is a snake, I shall cast her into the sea." An erotic maniac wrote next to that motto: "Woman is a treasure, I shall embrace her in my bosom."

A heartbroken person said angrily:

"Is it really that women are so lovely, that love is so sweet, that one must offer gold and kneel down to purchase it?... I don't believe there are so many foolish people in this world who are always happy to chain themselves into slavery and love those money-worshiping women..."

Are men and women so unequal? Especially among the bourgeoisie!

A notice posted in front of the gymnasium of the "University Hall" reads: "Those wearing leather shoes are not allowed to enter." After this dignified notice was posted, the result was: the male students obediently measured themselves before running into the gymnasium to see if they had changed into flat shoes. As for the princesses in the Eastern Palace? They have not yet given up their high heels. Alas! Same leather shoes, two different views, what injustice in the world is greater than this?

It is said that this is similar to Ah Q's love; the toad wants to eat swan meat, but he insists on telling people: "I don't like this girl at all!" Actually, this is the same as the fox not being able to get grapes and saying the grapes are sour anyway.

Generally, newly married women are all apprehensive about being abandoned by men and falling into suffering. A Japanese haiku writes very well, which can be used to describe the groaning complaints of women in our country today:

"To make him like me,"

This was the wish of the past.

The current worry is:

"How to avoid being abandoned by him."

A poet with rich emotions said:

"What is love? It is a faint, elusive thing, like viewing distant mountain scenery, as beautiful as a painting in the sky, but when you trek forward, it avoids you... "

Scattered Notes from Yi Palace 220

— Mizu

The God of Spring drove away the severe cold of the remaining winter. On the ground and branches, one can faintly see tender green buds and thin grass, and the warm breeze brings infinite vitality.

Yi Palace, surrounded by the atmosphere of spring, appears particularly inviting.

In front of it, there is a wide road. Short holly trees, as green as oil, stand on both sides of the road. Facing the palace gate, there is a cluster of small trees. Not far to the left, there is a wisteria trellis. The trellis is so long, with a thatched pavilion built in the center of the corridor. Some couples whisper sweet words here, and some discuss academic papers together.

The architecture of Yi Palace is very novel. Its overall shape resembles a concave character. The three-story Western-style buildings are all painted in goose yellow. Viewed in the morning light or evening glow, each has different colors. Especially at night, the neat rows of electric lights illuminate it so brilliantly. Seen from the incomplete Yi Yi Road piled with sand and dust, it is truly like a jade palace in the sky.

Inside the concave shape, there is a flat platform. Three sides of the platform have bamboo fences, and wisteria vines climb on the bamboo fences. Red, yellow, and purple flowers bloom very adorably, especially during the late spring and autumn seasons.

Entering through the palace gate, the reception desk is on the right. The entrance to the reception desk and the wall opposite it are covered with colorful notices, announcements, declarations, or book introductions, interspersed with small notes for lost items waiting to be claimed, or urgent meeting convocations regarding the Japanese pirates.

Further inside is the reception room. There are corridors on both sides. The clear steel windows provide ample light. The curtains covering the windows are half-open and half-closed. In the middle of the room, there is a large round table, surrounded by many chairs. In the four corners, there are four rattan round tables, each surrounded by four rattan chairs. Every day after 5 pm, or on Sundays and Saturday afternoons, there is probably not a single empty chair in the reception room.

At one point, many students proposed to open it, but they were still disappointed.

Dance 221

— Qun

Spring in Shanghai, youthful flames are active in the oblique, cold wind.

The night of the city, the pursuit of red lights and flesh. I was sent from the dreamlike Risheng Building to Guizhou Road. Groups of urban animals were sent into the pleasure exchange under the jade-like white thighs of beauties.

I was stuffed in the crowd, forgetting myself. Dance, the performance of flesh. I subconsciously reached into the pocket of my worn-out suit. The red lights extinguished their radiance. The urban animals turned into the black velvet door. The "eight corners" under the ticket booth had not lost their authority; and at the same time, the brass frame of "full upstairs and downstairs" also reflected in my eyes.

The servant in the royal uniform gave me a weak glance, like surprise, like contempt, lightly whispering to each other.

Ghostly music came from a very far place. I glanced at the jade-like white thighs of the beauties for the last time, and hurriedly fled out.

thighs of beauties.

The night of the city, the pursuit of red lights and flesh.

Spring in Shanghai, youthful flames are active in the oblique, cold wind.

Western Night School 222

— Sheng Hong

Alas; Shanghai is really a place where there are no wonders, and countless dark curtains emerge. Just taking the advertisement as a layer, it is enough to make me, a newcomer, be greatly deceived.

The fact is like this. This semester, due to various difficulties, I had to temporarily drop out of school and study at home. However, studying at home is of course not able to satisfy my desire for academics. Therefore, I planned to enroll in night school to specialize. Just imagine, Shanghai is so big, and the establishment of night schools is like bamboo shoots after the rain. Night school recruitment advertisements almost occupy the entire page in major newspaper advertising columns. Perhaps this is the popularization of Chinese education. These advertisements really speak like flowers falling from the sky, greatly praising themselves. To tear down the magic mirror, they are nothing more than high-class wild chickens. At first, I carefully looked around, and no school made me feel quite satisfied. Suddenly, an advertisement as big as a teacup attracted me: "Western 囗囗 English Special Night School" Next to it, a small line of attached notice was: "This school hires the current 囗囗" University professor, Western 囗囗, PhD as 囗-level professor" This is amazing. A night school would pay such a price to hire Professor 囗囗, PhD from University 囗囗 as a professor. That would naturally arouse my great attention. So, I immediately asked for a copy of the regulations to read carefully. This copy of the regulations, of course, said it like flowers falling from the sky, greatly boasting and drumming up, just like the advertisement. The tuition fee is only 18 yuan per semester, and the time is two hours every night. The books made me feel very satisfied. In this way, I resolutely paid the tuition fee and bought the books, and went to school the next night to attend classes.

The teacher on the first night was Cantonese. I was greatly shocked in my heart. Who knew I waited two nights, two nights, three nights, and the dreamed-of Western Professor 囗囗, PhD from University 囗囗 was like a needle sinking into the sea, and there was no news forever, and the time was also greatly wrong. The teacher was late to school until 7:20, and was full of "damn," and dismissed the class at 8:25, which was the opposite of the "two hours every night" stated in the regulations.

"Sir, who is the Doctor 囗囗" mentioned in your school's regulations? Also, the books mentioned in the regulations include Composition and Essay, Nest

Lied Grammar lv, Vicar of Wackfield,

and what else has not been taught?" One night, I could no longer bear it and questioned the Dean of Academic Affairs in this way.

Chain of Miscellaneous Thoughts 223

— Jiyu

Tune: Remembering Qin'e, first stanza

Heartbreak extreme, sorrow comes, fear to remember the Hu sky snow; Hu sky snow, long river flows swiftly, water sound sobbing.

Sound sobbing, general's good dream lost in butterflies; lost in butterflies, mountains and rivers broken, amorous feelings still hot.

Feelings still hot, men value righteousness, lightly leave; lightly leave, wind like shears, ambition like iron.

Heart like iron, sing a song, Guanshan black; Guanshan black, lone army suddenly strikes, close combat.

Combat joined, Hu machine gun fires, falling and scattering; falling and scattering, head falls to the ground, still calling to annihilate the thieves.

Calling to annihilate the thieves, Hu children emboldened, courage should crack; courage should crack, heartbreaking is, border soldiers sneak retreat.

Soldiers sneak retreat, border town overnight, color sullied; color sullied, three armies weep bitterly, bear to teach bowl to be broken!

Teach bowl to be broken, cast aside city, abandon land, whole wives and concubines; whole wives and concubines, general is wrong, who has no family?

No family, sacrifice body to resist tyranny, lightly cast aside; lightly cast aside, line by line, gradually far, northern wind biting cold.

Wind biting cold, bleak Sai grass meets the wind, broken; meets the wind, broken, yellow sand ten thousand miles, long river ice-bound.

River ice-bound, fluttering, filling the eye, reed catkin white; reed catkin white, connecting sky armor tents, disorderly blows, horn.

Blows horn, Hu flute sound, army heart anxious; army heart anxious, machine guns compete, shoot, residual limbs compete, fall.

Limbs compete, fall, leaning on saddle, resting on sword, look at bright moon; look at bright moon, boudoir in this night, ethereal soul flies over.

Soul flies over, lovesickness sleepless, blanket embraces knee; blanket embraces knee, fragrant heart secretly prays, Han soldiers early triumph!

Soldiers early triumph, Pingchuan how much, men's blood? Men's blood, generals offer land, righteous army exposed bones.

Army exposed bones, all people have death, what to regret? What to regret, because surrender is rewarded, this heart breaks extreme!

Self-Employment Introduction

Mr. Mei, a native of Wuxian, Jiangsu, 20 years old, middle school education, former trainee at Citibank, now willing to work as a trainee in a company or bank, or as a movie actor, etc., monthly salary must be above 15 yuan, address: Mr. Song Ji, No. 1013, Siwen Lane, Xinzha Road, this city.

Feng Yunsong, 24 years old, graduated from high school teachers, former teacher of Chinese, arithmetic, history, and geography in schools and secretary in military and political organs, now intends to solicit part-time work from 6 to 10 pm every day, remuneration is not counted, but must be similar to the above-mentioned nature of the job. Address: Yun Yongxing, Dong Wuchang Road, this city, forwarded.

Shop Assistant Communication

The More I'm Advised, the More Heartbroken I Become 224

— Lin Lanmei

Dear Editor:

I am a weak woman, 20 years of age. I also studied in elementary school for a few years, but due to economic reasons, I couldn't go on to higher education, and I'm always at home taking care of housework. Every time I think about finding something to do; either the location is too bad, with the risk of being insulted, so I'm unwilling to compromise myself, or their qualifications are too high, such as a university degree, a middle school degree, etc., rejecting me from a thousand miles away. There are two parents in my family who are over 60 years old, with no older siblings above and no younger siblings below, and no one to rely on. In this era of high cost of living, I feel very acute pressure every day. If I think about the future of the three of us who depend on each other for life, it really makes you restless! Seeing those leisurely people enjoying themselves every day, how can I not be both envious and jealous?

The year before last, through a classmate's introduction, I met a Mr. Luo. He fits my ideal very well and loves me very much. He once proposed to me, and at that time, I was willing in my heart, but thinking about "Without me, what would my parents do for the rest of their years?", I was speechless, and tears fell like rain. He was confused, and after repeated questioning, I had to tell him sincerely: I said, "I myself have no conditions, the most important thing is, are you willing to take care of my parents in the end?" Hearing these words, his face was troubled, and after a long pause, he said, "Unfortunately, I am also a man with a hard life, and my monthly salary is very limited; I also have an old mother and a weak younger sibling who rely on me to support them." Therefore, our marriage had to be painfully severed. Since then, he has often said, "I hope that my monthly income will one day increase to a considerable amount, and we can still get married." Now? Because he couldn't resist his old mother's opinion, he married another woman last winter. Hearing this news, I felt like a prisoner hearing the judge announce his death sentence in court, and I couldn't express my suffering. Until now, Mr. Luo still often sends letters to comfort me and advise me not to be too sad; but I, the more I'm advised, the more heartbroken I become. Alas!

Dear Editor, people are born equal, and I haven't done anything wrong, why do I have to suffer so much? Is it really a matter of a previous life? (omitted below)

Sincerely, Lin Lanmei

Editor's Note: After reading Ms. Lin's letter, you can't help but feel a sourness in your nose; her life is so pitiful. Therefore, even though she is not a shop employee, worker, or apprentice, we have to discuss it publicly here.

It is true that "people are born equal." However, this is "a kind of proposition, opinion, ideal only. Ancient and modern, Chinese and foreign," has never been realized. Some people are born rich and noble, and some people are born poor and lowly. But this is definitely not a matter of a previous life, it is caused by the evil capitalism. We demand equality, and blaming heaven and earth is useless. We should attack this evil society, that is the way out.

Ms. Lin's standard for choosing a husband is to find a man who can take care of her parents to the end, which is difficult! Now the cost of living is getting higher every day, and a man who supports a wife is already covered in sweat, so "the call for women to have the ability to be independent" can be heard everywhere; how can they still have the ability to take care of your parents? It is your filial piety to support your parents, which is admirable, but you can only offer your own mental strength to fulfill this wish. In today's society, it is really not easy to find a husband to take care of your parents! Even if there are some wealthy young masters who can take on this responsibility, then you will inevitably be angry for life! As for women's occupations, some of course require considerable qualifications, but there are also some that do not require very profound knowledge. Speaking of some positions, although there is a risk of being insulted, as long as you are firm, you are not afraid. So, we advise Ms. Lin to quickly find something to do and use the price she gets to support her parents. Marriage is another issue. Don't mix the issue of supporting parents into it. Mr. Luo already has a wife, and it's impossible to salvage; but a second Mr. Luo is not difficult to find again, so there is no need to be too sad. I don't know if this advice will make you even more heartbroken!

Novel

Coal Hill (Continued) 225

— Written by Ed Falkowiki, Abridged and Translated by Zhixiang

"Don't talk like that, Peter. We've lived here for a long time. Now, where can we go?"

Peter remained silent. He placed his cold pipe in the iron ashtray.

You are right, Mary! In all respects, I show the appearance of old age; tonight, I have dressed up to go out. It's been a long time since I last met my companions. It's Saturday night, and I want to go out and have some fun, no matter what."

Although smoking is forbidden, drinking is still allowed. Everyone at home can drink as much as they want! Or they can increase it at will!

The Jiggai Cafe on Sino-Western Street is often frequented by people. It seems to boast of exclusive business. The next room is full of traveling salesmen, private wine merchants, and painted prostitutes. They are all trying to have fun as much as possible.

The managers and foremen in the mines drink in the Peisike shop on Coal Street. Merchants who contract materials in the mines come there to invite foremen to eat and drink, and they won't blame the merchants for wasting. They like such waste. We should know that this is the secret to doing business! Entertainment expenses are equal to investment in sales. If you are willing to waste like this, you can win the favor of the managers, and their favor is the price of increasing the value of various materials.

The workers often live in the tunnels of the mines. There, they fight desperately with the ore, and the reward they get is only some coal. How would they know that this Peisike shop, poor workers! How many eras will it take for a worker to become an intellectual in America!

Notice

Regarding the Coal Hill novel, on the previous two days, the signature "Sui" was actually a misunderstanding, and there are also places in the original text that have been deleted, so now it has been changed to "Translated and interpreted by Zhixiang," and this is specifically stated;

Movie Special Issue

The Past and Future of Soviet Films 226

— Huang Junru

Since the Shanghai Grand Theatre screened the Soviet sound film "Road to Life" this time, it has aroused the Sensafi of the general public in Shanghai.

The reason for this is not only because the film has a unique style, which is different from the American film style that has always advocated hedonism, but also because it can point out the way forward in life. But what is the current state of the film industry in the Soviet Union, and what is the situation of Soviet films exported abroad? I think this must also be something that the general public is eager to know. Therefore, I will briefly introduce its situation below:

(1) The Soviet Film New Five-Year Plan

Filmification, along with electrification, chemicalization, and automobilization, are all the main slogans of the current Soviet Union. Last year, the number of times Soviet residents watched movies averaged ten times per person. If we discuss it separately in urban and rural areas, it is 21 times in urban areas and 5-6 times in rural areas. In order to make the people closer to movies, the Soviet government plans to universalize the film network in the Second Five-Year Plan. It is expected to triple the number of cinemas in the Russian Republic, paying special attention to the areas of small and medium-sized ethnic groups, such as the Central Asian Kazakhstan within the Republic, which will increase the number of cinemas by six and a half times; newly established 42,244 film clubs; state-owned agricultural centers, etc., building 310 of the latest modern movie theaters; labor farmers' clubs, etc., all equipped with film projectors. It is estimated that in 1937, the final year of the Second Five-Year Plan, the total number of movie viewers in the entire Federation will reach 3 billion. The number of viewers will be 48 times per adult, which is compared with the end of the First Five-Year Plan as follows: 1932 1937

City 21 times 56 times

Rural 5-6 times 41 times

It can be seen from this that the Second Five-Year Plan is not only to increase the number of viewers from an average of 10 times to 48 times, but also to gradually bring the number of viewers closer together in urban and rural areas. (2) The Soviet Union's Film Export Volume

Although Soviet films are quite popular with audiences in various countries due to their unique themes and techniques, they cannot obtain the freedom of public import due to the ideological content often touching the taboos of censorship in various countries; and because the rental fees are quite high, the export volume has not yet reached the maximum number. Last year, from January to September, its export volume was only 59,000 rubles (weight 2 tons), an increase of 25,000 rubles compared to 34,000 rubles (weight 1 ton) in 1931.

Director Bao Caiqi's [Love in the Battlefield] 227

— Guo Shenghong

Indeed, Frank Bao Caiqi's [Seventh Heaven] made a profound impression on people around the world. As a result, he was elected as one of the world's top ten directors in 1931.

A few years ago, in response to the enthusiastic demands of movie fans around the world, he began directing [Love in the Battlefield], (A Farewell to Arms). The plot, like [Seventh Heaven], is full of sorrow and allure, with a touch of the color of the Russian literary giant Tolstoy's masterpiece [Resurrection]. The film depicts the sorrow of life's separations very deeply, and the whole film is immersed in sad music and melancholic emotions.

Regarding the leading role, Frank Bao Caiqi carefully selected the actors, as cautiously as Lubitsch selected the leading roles for [The Merry Widow]. As a result, Helen Hayes, who won the Academy Award for Best Actress the year before last, was selected. The male lead is the veteran star Gary Cooper, with Adolphe Menjou. The plot is so mournful, lingering, and tearful, truly touching people's hearts. The general idea is about a military officer who meets a young woman in a certain village, and they fall in love that night. Soon after, the officer goes to the front line to fight, and the woman gives birth to a child at home, who unfortunately dies young. The woman waits for the officer to return, but there is no news. The woman becomes ill from accumulated worry, and is on her deathbed. At this time, the officer suddenly returns from the front line. The woman only slightly opens her almond eyes at the moment of parting, giving the officer a slight bitter smile, and her fragrant soul flutters away. It is truly [Heaven and earth may pass away, but this sorrow will last forever]!

Further Introduction to [A Pair of Ill-Fated Lovers] 228

— Ping Chen

Coming Soon to the New Guang Theater

Chinese people embrace familism, and their concern for succession is particularly strong. They often scrimp and save, working hard all their lives like beasts of burden, to leave this property for their children and grandchildren to use. Such people are truly foolish!

The Japanese have invaded Yuguan, and the volunteer army is desperately fighting, enduring hunger and cold. The plight of the refugees from the Northeast is completely irrelevant to the wealthy. They are preparing to pass on their huge family fortunes to their children and grandchildren, and are unwilling to donate even a little to the volunteer army or refugees. As for whether their children and grandchildren will be spendthrifts or slaves to a conquered nation in the future, they will not think about it!

Tianyi Film Company's new sound production [A Pair of Ill-Fated Lovers], its central idea is to depict the evils of inheritance. It clearly tells us that inheritance for children is [not only useless but also harmful]. At the same time, it also tells us that the wealthy should use their wealth to establish social enterprises to benefit the masses.

[A Pair of Ill-Fated Lovers] is a realistic depiction, a powerful film aimed at the ills of Chinese society. Another point worth mentioning is that several of the sets in [A Pair of Ill-Fated Lovers] are indeed worthy of the description [magnificent and luxurious].

Jiang Qing, Returned from Hollywood

The roles played by Mary Doran in Hollywood are those of kind old women, so everyone calls her [Mother on the Screen]. But she has been in the industry for more than 20 years, and many people expect her to retire soon.

Jackie Coogan is known as a child prodigy, but he is very naughty. Once, he cut many small holes in his newly made shirt, but he wore it to the streets. This is one page of his humorous history. However, he has been much quieter recently, because he has declared that he will withdraw from the film industry and go to state university.

Mary Pickford cut her golden long hair three years ago and turned it into a curly style, which she felt was very suitable for a young woman's dress.

Douglas Fairbanks loves to practice hunting and shooting. Whenever he is drunk, he always talks about his martial arts skills. He has recently traveled the world, his footprints all over the world. The American Film Institute selected him as the star who traveled the most in 1932.

After Charlie Chaplin's [City Lights] was released, he still firmly adhered to his film production principles. He is very interested in shooting a film about [Napoleon Bonaparte], but it is still undecided. He may still serve as the screenwriter, director, and leading actor himself.

Charlie Farrell's only hobby is collecting old things, stamps, old coins, treasures, and the like. He also likes Chinese embroidery very much. He said that the Chinese are very easy to trade with.

Anna May Wong, a Chinese actress, is touring Europe. She seems to be tired of her film career. When someone asked her if she would return to her motherland, she just smiled.

A scene from Tianyi Film Company's new sound film [A Pair of Ill-Fated Lovers]

Talking about Li Lili 229

— Yun

Presumably everyone knows that the new stars in the film industry,

Wang Renmei and Li Lili are the mainstays of the Bright Moon Troupe!

When they performed on stage at the Bright Moon Troupe, I wrote some articles, which may have contained some opportunistic elements!

She!! Li Lili!! was born in Beiping. She can speak very clear and fluent Mandarin. When she was twelve years old, she came to Shanghai from Beiping to seek her new life. At that time, she worshiped Li Jinhui as her adoptive father. Her real surname is Qian, and her father, Qian Zhuzhuang, is a doctor in Beiping. She only changed her surname to Li after becoming Li Jinhui's adopted daughter. As for why she doesn't have the surname Qian, that is a mysterious matter.

She and Wang Renmei were recruited by the United China Singing and Dancing Troupe at the same time. When the United China Singing and Dancing Troupe performed publicly, she met us several times. Last year, when the United China Singing and Dancing Troupe disbanded, she also followed Wang Renmei's example and appeared on the screen. Her debut work was [Blood of Love in the Volcano]. After the release of this film, she got the nickname [Beauty Essence] (which is opposed to Wang Renmei's nickname [Beauty King]). Later, some people called her [Sweetheart]. Her second film in United China was the recently released [Dawn]. But all of these were silent films. We heard her sweet voice on the screen only from Tianyi's [Poetry on the Banana Plant].

She is only eighteen years old this year, which is the age of a young woman.
